# Yoda

< [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda")

[Edit](/wiki/Yoda/Legends?veaction=edit) 

* [Edit source](/wiki/Yoda/Legends?action=edit)
* [History](/wiki/Yoda/Legends?action=history)
* [Purge](/wiki/Yoda/Legends?action=purge)

[896 BBY](/wiki/896_BBY/Legends "896 BBY/Legends") ([861BrS](/wiki/Great_ReSynchronization "Great ReSynchronization"))[[1]](#cite_note-Jedi_vs._Sith-1)

### Died

[4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY/Legends "4 ABY/Legends") (39:3), [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah/Legends "Dagobah/Legends")[[2]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_VI:_Return_of_the_Jedi-2)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Character)

:   "*Size matters not. Look at me. Judge me by my size, do you? Hmm? Hmm. And well you should not. For my ally is the Force, and a powerful ally it is. Life creates it, makes it grow. Its energy surrounds us and binds us. Luminous beings are we, not this crude matter. You must feel the Force around you; here, between you, me, the tree, the rock, everywhere, yes. Even between the land and the ship.*"
:   ―Yoda, to Luke Skywalker — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Yoda-SizeMattersNot-Full.flac/revision/latest?cb=20251220050900)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Yoda-SizeMattersNot-Full.flac "File:Yoda-SizeMattersNot-Full.flac"))[[4]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_V:_The_Empire_Strikes_Back-4)

**Yoda**, considered by some to be the **Avatar of Light**, was a [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive/Legends "Force-sensitive/Legends") [male](/wiki/Gender/Legends "Gender/Legends") [being](/wiki/Species/Legends "Species/Legends") of a [mysterious species](/wiki/Yoda%27s_species/Legends "Yoda's species/Legends"), one of the most legendary, renowned and powerful [Jedi Masters](/wiki/Jedi_Master/Legends "Jedi Master/Legends") in [galactic history](/wiki/Timeline_of_galactic_history/Legends "Timeline of galactic history/Legends"). He was known for his legendary wisdom, mastery of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force/Legends "The Force/Legends") and skills in [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat/Legends "Lightsaber combat/Legends"). Yoda served as a member of the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council/Legends "Jedi High Council/Legends") in the last [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century/Legends "Standard century/Legends") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Legends "Galactic Republic/Legends") and as [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master/Legends "Grand Master/Legends") oversaw the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order/Legends "Jedi Order/Legends") before, during, and after the devastating [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars/Legends "Clone Wars/Legends"). Following the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis/Legends "First Battle of Geonosis/Legends"), Yoda held the title of [Master of the Order](/wiki/Master_of_the_Order/Legends "Master of the Order/Legends") in addition to that of Grand Master. In his centuries of service to [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy/Legends "The galaxy/Legends") and the Force, Grand Master Yoda had a hand in the training of nearly all the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi/Legends "Jedi/Legends") in the Order, including such luminaries as [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi/Legends "Obi-Wan Kenobi/Legends"), [Ki-Adi-Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi/Legends "Ki-Adi-Mundi/Legends") and [Oppo Rancisis](/wiki/Oppo_Rancisis/Legends "Oppo Rancisis/Legends"), all of whom would come to serve on the Jedi Council along with him.

Standing about 66 cm tall, Yoda was a [male](/wiki/Gender/Legends "Gender/Legends") member of a [mysterious species](/wiki/Yoda%27s_species/Legends "Yoda's species/Legends"), details of which he did not reveal. Yoda served as a member of the Jedi Order for centuries, eventually gaining a seat on the Jedi High Council, before reigning as the Grand Master of the Jedi. He had exceptional skills in lightsaber combat, having mastered all forms and stances of lightsaber combat, except the Vaapad subset of [Form VII](/wiki/Form_VII/Legends "Form VII/Legends") (he had mastered the original Form VII variant known as Juyo), but known for being particularly accomplished in [Form IV](/wiki/Form_IV/Legends "Form IV/Legends"), often employing the acrobatic techniques of the form. Many considered him a [swordmaster](/wiki/Swordmaster "Swordmaster") and the greatest duelist in the Jedi Order, even surpassing [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu/Legends "Mace Windu/Legends") and [Count](/wiki/Count/Legends "Count/Legends") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku/Legends "Dooku/Legends").

Though arguably the Order's greatest master of the Force and most skilled warrior, Yoda believed most firmly in the importance of instructing younger generations and never missed an opportunity to ensure his students learn from their experiences. At heart, the diminutive Jedi Master was a teacher; indeed, he instructed nearly all the Jedi in the order, to some extent, during his reign as Grand Master.[[11]](#cite_note-Yoda:_Dark_Rendezvous-11)

Though Yoda was, arguably, the most highly Force-attuned member of the Order, he was not flawless. It was partially due to his failure to recognize that [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor/Legends "Supreme Chancellor/Legends") [Palpatine](/wiki/Palpatine/Legends "Palpatine/Legends") was actually responsible for the outbreak of the Clone Wars, and was in fact the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord/Legends "Sith Lord/Legends") Darth Sidious, or to destroy him in battle, that the Republic was overthrown and the Jedi Order decimated. The Grand Master was among the few Jedi to survive Darth Sidious' [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge/Legends "Great Jedi Purge/Legends"), after the beginning of which, he went into exile on the swamp planet of [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah/Legends "Dagobah/Legends").

Later, before [dying](/wiki/Death/Legends "Death/Legends") and becoming one with the Force in [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY/Legends "4 ABY/Legends"), the exiled Jedi Master was responsible for the instruction of [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker/Legends "Luke Skywalker/Legends"), who would use Yoda's training as a basis for the creation of a [New Jedi Order](/wiki/New_Jedi_Order "New Jedi Order"), after defeating the Sith. Following his death, Master Yoda [retained his identity](/wiki/Force_ghost/Legends "Force ghost/Legends") within the Force and was revered as amongst the most legendary Jedi Masters of all time by Skywalker's reconstituted Order.

## Biography[]

### Early life[]

:   "*A trial of being old is this: remembering which thing one has said into which young ears.*"
:   ―Yoda[[11]](#cite_note-Yoda:_Dark_Rendezvous-11)

 [![A young Yoda being trained by  ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/GormoTrainingYoda.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130815140924) [![A young Yoda being trained by  ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/GormoTrainingYoda.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130815140924)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/GormoTrainingYoda.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130815140924) 

A young Yoda being trained by [Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master/Legends "Jedi Master/Legends") [Gormo](/wiki/N%27Kata_Del_Gormo/Legends "N'Kata Del Gormo/Legends")

 

Very little is known about Yoda's early life. He was from a remote planet, but which one remains a mystery.[[12]](#cite_note-Legendary-12) According to one legend,[[8]](#cite_note-Twitter-8) Yoda originally did not know that he was [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive/Legends "Force-sensitive/Legends") at all.[[7]](#cite_note-Nine-7)[[12]](#cite_note-Legendary-12) His path towards the Jedi began when he left his home [planet](/wiki/Planet/Legends "Planet/Legends")[[7]](#cite_note-Nine-7)[[12]](#cite_note-Legendary-12) with a [Human](/wiki/Human/Legends "Human/Legends") [friend](/wiki/Unidentified_Force-sensitive_Human "Unidentified Force-sensitive Human"), who also did not know he was Force-sensitive,[[7]](#cite_note-Nine-7) on an old, barely space-worthy ship en route to the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds/Legends "Core Worlds/Legends") to seek employment.[[7]](#cite_note-Nine-7)[[12]](#cite_note-Legendary-12) However, long before they could reach their destination, the ship was struck by a large asteroid, causing it to become severely disabled beyond their abilities to repair. They spent several days drifting dead in space during which time both their life support systems and rations came close to being exhausted, and there was still no response to their distress signal. It seemed like they would soon meet their deaths until their sensors picked up a [star system](/wiki/Star_system/Legends "Star system/Legends") not too far away. They had just enough power to make it there, and did so before crash landing on a strange[[7]](#cite_note-Nine-7)I[[12]](#cite_note-Legendary-12) [swampy planet](/wiki/Unidentified_swamp_planet "Unidentified swamp planet") covered with a dense fog.[[7]](#cite_note-Nine-7)

They spent a few days there before being found by a strange being: [Hysalrian](/wiki/Hysalrian/Legends "Hysalrian/Legends") Jedi Master [N'Kata Del Gormo](/wiki/N%27Kata_Del_Gormo/Legends "N'Kata Del Gormo/Legends"), who revealed to them both that they were very much Force-sensitive.[[7]](#cite_note-Nine-7) The Jedi Master invited Yoda to become his apprentice, also known as a [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan/Legends "Padawan/Legends").[[12]](#cite_note-Legendary-12) Master Gormo took them to his home, where he trained them in the ways of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force/Legends "The Force/Legends") and, not long after their training was complete, a [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic/Legends "Galactic Republic/Legends") [starship](/wiki/Starship/Legends "Starship/Legends") picked up their distress signal and rescued the two friends, who were now [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi/Legends "Jedi/Legends") themselves. Departing the world, Yoda went to [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant/Legends "Coruscant/Legends"), where he continued his training at the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple/Legends "Jedi Temple/Legends") as a [Jedi Initiate](/wiki/Jedi_Initiate/Legends "Jedi Initiate/Legends").[[7]](#cite_note-Nine-7) As time passed, he proved to be a skilled Jedi,[[12]](#cite_note-Legendary-12) and he studied under the Jedi Master [Fae Coven](/wiki/Fae_Coven "Fae Coven").[[13]](#cite_note-The_Jedi_Path-13) Eventually, Yoda passed [The Gathering](/wiki/Gathering/Legends "Gathering/Legends") and was assisted by the [architect droid](/wiki/Architect_droid/Legends "Architect droid/Legends") [Huyang](/wiki/Huyang/Legends "Huyang/Legends") in the construction of his first lightsaber.[[14]](#cite_note-A_Necessary_Bond-14)[[7]](#cite_note-Nine-7)

### Jedi Master[]

:   "*Secret, shall I tell you? Grand Master of Jedi Order am I. Won this job in a raffle I did, think you? 'How did you know, how did you know, Master Yoda?' Master Yoda knows these things. His job it is.*"
:   ―Yoda[[11]](#cite_note-Yoda:_Dark_Rendezvous-11)

When Yoda had completed his Padawan training, he became a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight/Legends "Jedi Knight/Legends"), meaning he could go on important missions. By the age of 96, he had become a Jedi Master. Later, he was elected to join the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council/Legends "Jedi High Council/Legends").[[12]](#cite_note-Legendary-12) By [800 BBY](/wiki/800_BBY/Legends "800 BBY/Legends"), Yoda had begun the training of his first student, who would be one of the many Padawans Yoda would train over the long centuries of his life.

 [![Yoda with Jedi Knight Dooku](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/Once_Allies_SWG4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120611222547) [![Yoda with Jedi Knight Dooku](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/Once_Allies_SWG4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20120611222547)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/48/Once_Allies_SWG4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120611222547) 

Yoda with Jedi Knight Dooku

 

Later, Yoda became one of the Jedi Masters who led the mobile academy aboard the starship *[Chu'unthor](/wiki/Chu%27unthor "Chu'unthor")*, which was constructed circa [500 BBY](/wiki/500_BBY/Legends "500 BBY/Legends"). After crash-landing on the planet of [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir/Legends "Dathomir/Legends") at around [230 BBY](/wiki/230_BBY/Legends "230 BBY/Legends"), Yoda and the other Jedi fought with the famed [Witches of Dathomir](/wiki/Nightsisters/Legends "Nightsisters/Legends"). Coming to a stalemate, he agreed to leave the ship's data tapes. Although he left no means of reading the tapes, they were bestowed to [Rell](/wiki/Rell_(Dathomir) "Rell (Dathomir)") of the [Singing Mountain Clan](/wiki/Singing_Mountain_Clan "Singing Mountain Clan") for safekeeping until such a time, Yoda foresaw, when a Jedi would come to save the planet from darkness and the information could safely be shared with the Witches. This did not happen until around [8 ABY](/wiki/8_ABY/Legends "8 ABY/Legends"), when Yoda's final student, [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker/Legends "Luke Skywalker/Legends"), found his way to Dathomir, fulfilling his Master's prophecy.[[15]](#cite_note-TheCourtshipOfPrincessLeia-15)

Yoda once traveled to [Kushibah](/wiki/Kushibah "Kushibah") in search of a new Padawan. There among the diminutive [Kushiban](/wiki/Kushiban "Kushiban"), the Jedi Master discovered young [Ikrit](/wiki/Ikrit "Ikrit"), who proved strong in the Force, and took him to be trained as a Jedi. As a Jedi Knight, Ikrit once lost control during a petty disagreement and almost murdered a friend with his lightsaber, with Yoda risking his own life to stop him. As a result, Ikrit forsook the use of lightsabers for years afterward.[[16]](#cite_note-Vader's_Fortress-16)

By around [400 BBY](/wiki/400_BBY/Legends "400 BBY/Legends"), when [Beldorion](/wiki/Beldorion "Beldorion") left the Jedi Order, Yoda could be considered one of the greatest Masters in Jedi history, comparable with [Nomi Sunrider](/wiki/Nomi_Sunrider "Nomi Sunrider") or [Thon](/wiki/Thon "Thon"), both of whom had lived more than 3,500 years earlier.[[17]](#cite_note-Planet_of_Twilight-17)

By [200 BBY](/wiki/200_BBY/Legends "200 BBY/Legends"), Yoda, along with other Jedi Masters of that time, discovered that the shape of the Force had begun to flux, becoming murky and uncertain. Studying the perplexing mystery in silent meditation, the Jedi High Council, of which Yoda was now a senior member, was unanimous: the power of the [dark side](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Dark side of the Force/Legends") was growing. While the Council and the other Jedi believed this indicated the growing power of the [Sith](/wiki/Sith/Legends "Sith/Legends") or other dark-siders, Yoda put forth the possibility that the darkening of the Force might suggest the imminent approach of the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One/Legends "Chosen One/Legends"), which prophecy said would bring balance to the Force. In opposition to this theory, several of the younger Jedi disputed Yoda's findings, and formed a breakaway sect—the [Potentium](/wiki/Potentium "Potentium"). Their heresy was not welcomed by the Council, and Yoda led the campaign to expel them from the order in [130 BBY](/wiki/130_BBY "130 BBY").[[11]](#cite_note-Yoda:_Dark_Rendezvous-11)

Around one hundred and fifty [years](/wiki/Standard_year/Legends "Standard year/Legends") before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars/Legends "Clone Wars/Legends"), Yoda traveled to [Ord Cestus](/wiki/Ord_Cestus/Legends "Ord Cestus/Legends") and saved the native [X'Ting](/wiki/X%27Ting "X'Ting") from disaster. They honored Yoda by building a giant statue of him, at least 70 meters tall, inside the [X'Ting Hall of Heroes](/wiki/X%27Ting_Hall_of_Heroes "X'Ting Hall of Heroes").[[18]](#cite_note-The_Hive-18) At some point between [133 BBY](/wiki/133_BBY/Legends "133 BBY/Legends") and [69 BBY](/wiki/69_BBY/Legends "69 BBY/Legends"), Master Yoda attempted to see the future of [Byrch Dyshkava](/wiki/Byrch_Dyshkava "Byrch Dyshkava"), a Padawan who had mysteriously gone missing after a mission. Yoda failed to provide the Order with any useful information.[[19]](#cite_note-BL-19)

In [102 BBY](/wiki/102_BBY/Legends "102 BBY/Legends") an infant by the name of [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku/Legends "Dooku/Legends"), heir to the title of [Count](/wiki/Count/Legends "Count/Legends") on the planet of [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno/Legends "Serenno/Legends"), was discovered by the Jedi and willingly given to the Order by his parents. When Dooku reached the appropriate age, he was taken as a Padawan by Council member [Thame Cerulian](/wiki/Thame_Cerulian "Thame Cerulian"). However, even though he studied under Cerulian, Yoda took a particular interest in the young Dooku and was frequently his adviser and confidant. The Jedi Master, however, was equally quick to point out Dooku's flaws when necessary. Yoda assisted quite closely in Dooku's lightsaber training as a Padawan, and building from this foundation, Dooku became an accomplished duelist with the weapon. In Dooku's later years, only Yoda and senior Council member [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu/Legends "Mace Windu/Legends") were considered equal to his skill with a lightsaber. Later, Yoda also served as the lightsaber instructor of [Cin Drallig](/wiki/Cin_Drallig/Legends "Cin Drallig/Legends"), who would become the [Battlemaster](/wiki/Battlemaster/Legends "Battlemaster/Legends") of the Jedi Temple.

### Yinchorri uprising ([33 BBY](/wiki/33_BBY/Legends "33 BBY/Legends"))[]

#### Early engagements[]

 [![Yoda and the Council learn of the Yinchorri uprising.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/Mayvitch_soldier_contacting_Jedi.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150620222629) [![Yoda and the Council learn of the Yinchorri uprising.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/Mayvitch_soldier_contacting_Jedi.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150620222629)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/73/Mayvitch_soldier_contacting_Jedi.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150620222629) 

Yoda and the Council learn of the Yinchorri uprising.

 

In [33 BBY](/wiki/33_BBY/Legends "33 BBY/Legends"), the Jedi Council received a transmission sent four standard days earlier informing them of an [attack on Mayvitch 7](/wiki/Battle_of_Mayvitch_7 "Battle of Mayvitch 7") instigated by the [Yinchorri](/wiki/Yinchorri/Legends "Yinchorri/Legends"). After news of this reached [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor/Legends "Supreme Chancellor/Legends") [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum/Legends "Finis Valorum/Legends"), he asked Mace Windu to send Jedi to negotiate with the Yinchorri. However, the aggressive Yinchorri murdered the two Jedi sent to negotiate and sent their mutilated bodies to Valorum's [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant/Legends "Coruscant/Legends") doorstep as a warning.[[20]](#cite_note-ActsOfWar-20)

Following this, the Council created a Jedi strike team of twelve, including senior Councilor Mace Windu, to the [Yinchorri system](/wiki/Yinchorri_system "Yinchorri system"). Reports of the Jedi's engagement with Yinchorri forces that reached Yoda and the Council proved confusing and contradictory, while the diminutive Jedi Master sensed danger coming toward him in the Force. Yoda's danger sense proved accurate when the Yinchorri launched a raid on the Jedi Temple.[[20]](#cite_note-ActsOfWar-20)

#### Raid on the Temple[]

The Yinchorri task force found that all the Jedi sleeping quarters were empty. The troops then entered a chamber where they were met by several armed Jedi, including Yoda. In the end, almost all the Yinchorri were killed, and two Jedi died: [Jude Rozess](/wiki/Jude_Rozess "Jude Rozess") and [Tieren Nie-Tan](/wiki/Tieren_Nie-Tan "Tieren Nie-Tan").[[20]](#cite_note-ActsOfWar-20)

 [![Yoda kills a Yinchorri warrior.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Yoda_Yinchorri.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150621043122) [![Yoda kills a Yinchorri warrior.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Yoda_Yinchorri.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20150621043122)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Yoda_Yinchorri.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150621043122) 

Yoda kills a Yinchorri warrior.

 

Yoda interrogated the last remaining Yinchorri and asked him the location of the Yinchorri high command. The soldier responded to the Jedi Master by telling him that he did not know since he was only an ordinary soldier. Yoda then turned to converse with [Soon Bayts](/wiki/Soon_Bayts "Soon Bayts"), a Jedi Knight who brought word from [Adi Gallia](/wiki/Adi_Gallia/Legends "Adi Gallia/Legends") and [Eeth Koth](/wiki/Eeth_Koth/Legends "Eeth Koth/Legends") that the high command was not on Yitheeth and that they were heading to Yibikkoror to help [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon/Legends "Plo Koon/Legends") and [Micah Giiett](/wiki/Micah_Giiett "Micah Giiett").[[20]](#cite_note-ActsOfWar-20)

These distractions gave the Yinchorri in the Temple enough time to grab his weapon and attempt to shoot the Jedi Master. Yoda, however, used the Force to throw him against a wall, killing him. The Jedi then came to the conclusion that the Yinchorri were misguided rather than bloodthirsty and that the attack may have been the work of an unknown party, rather than the Yinchorri themselves.[[20]](#cite_note-ActsOfWar-20)

#### Endgame[]

Following the unsuccessful raid on the Jedi Temple, the Jedi strike team continued to engage the Yinchorri, while Yoda remained on Coruscant. Master Windu eventually reported to Yoda, informing him that the strike team had discovered the location of the Yinchorri's high command, thanks to Master [Yaddle's](/wiki/Yaddle/Legends "Yaddle/Legends") knowledge of the [Jedi holocrons](/wiki/Holocron/Legends "Holocron/Legends"). The Jedi led an attack on the world, while four navy attack groups authorized by the Senate arrived to help them, concluding the uprising.[[20]](#cite_note-ActsOfWar-20)

### Invasion of Naboo ([32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY/Legends "32 BBY/Legends"))[]

:   "*There's no doubt. The mysterious warrior was a Sith.*"  
    "*Always two there are. No more, no less. A Master and an apprentice.*"  
    "*But which one was destroyed, the Master, or the Apprentice?*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Yoda, about Darth Maul — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/AlwaysTwoThereAre-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250407192606)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:AlwaysTwoThereAre-TPM.flac "File:AlwaysTwoThereAre-TPM.flac"))[[21]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace-21)

In [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY/Legends "32 BBY/Legends"), the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate/Legends "Galactic Senate/Legends") passed legislation that called for the taxation of trade routes to outlying systems, in an attempt to weaken the ever-expanding [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation/Legends "Trade Federation/Legends"), which had grown increasingly powerful—to the point that it had its own Senate delegation and easily "persuaded" Republic weapons inspectors to overlook the arming of the Federation's shipment vessels into lethal battleships.[[21]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace-21)

 [![Yoda during the Naboo crisis ()](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/Yoda_Episode_I_Canon.png/revision/latest?cb=20130921110620) [![Yoda during the Naboo crisis ()](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/Yoda_Episode_I_Canon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130921110620)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/Yoda_Episode_I_Canon.png/revision/latest?cb=20130921110620) 

Yoda during the Naboo crisis ([32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY/Legends "32 BBY/Legends"))

 

As such, the Federation created an invasion force of battle droids, in addition to their growing fleet of warships, and in protest of the Senate's legislation, blockaded the small world of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo/Legends "Naboo/Legends"). [Queen](/wiki/Queen/Legends "Queen/Legends") [Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala/Legends "Padmé Amidala/Legends") of Naboo implored the help of the Republic, and as such, Supreme Chancellor [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum/Legends "Finis Valorum/Legends") asked Yoda and the Council to send Jedi to negotiate with the Trade Federation, as ambassadors of the Republic.[[21]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace-21)

The Council sent Jedi Master [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn/Legends "Qui-Gon Jinn/Legends"), and his apprentice [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi/Legends "Obi-Wan Kenobi/Legends"), to negotiate with the leadership of the Trade Federation. However, upon the arrival of the Jedi, the Federation attempted to assassinate them and began invading Naboo; the Jedi were able to escape their would-be killers and rescue the Queen of Naboo, Amidala.[[21]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace-21)

Upon returning to Coruscant, Qui-Gon Jinn brought a young [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker/Legends "Anakin Skywalker/Legends") to the Jedi Council, requesting to train him once Obi-Wan Kenobi had completed the [trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials/Legends "Jedi Trials/Legends") necessary to become a Jedi Knight, as Jedi could only have one apprentice at a time. Yoda, as the teacher of many of those on the Council, and its most venerable and respected member, played a key role in that body's initial decision to deny the request. Yoda believed that the boy was clearly affected by his years as a slave and that he still clung too tightly to the memory of [his mother](/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars/Legends "Shmi Skywalker Lars/Legends") to be trained safely. The boy's future, Yoda thought, was clouded. Qui-Gon, however, continued to insist that Skywalker was the Chosen One, who would bring balance to the Force.[[21]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace-21)

#### Return of the Sith[]

:   "*The Sith were before Master Yoda's time, were they not, Master?*"  
    "*Nothing was before Yoda's time, Padawan.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Qui-Gon Jinn[[22]](#cite_note-CloakDeception-22)

In addition to this supposed Chosen One, Qui-Gon brought news of the return of the Sith; while he and the Queen's entourage had been preparing to depart the planet of [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine/Legends "Tatooine/Legends") after having their damaged ship repaired, [what appeared to be a Sith Lord](/wiki/Darth_Maul/Legends "Darth Maul/Legends") confronted the Jedi Master in a lightsaber duel.[[21]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace-21)

 [![Yoda makes Kenobi a Jedi Knight.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Obi-Wan_Knighted_Episode_I_Canon.png/revision/latest?cb=20130126035557) [![Yoda makes Kenobi a Jedi Knight.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Obi-Wan_Knighted_Episode_I_Canon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130126035557)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3c/Obi-Wan_Knighted_Episode_I_Canon.png/revision/latest?cb=20130126035557) 

Yoda makes Kenobi a Jedi Knight.

 

After finding the Senate unresponsive to her pleas for aid, Queen Amidala demanded a vote of no confidence in Supreme Chancellor Valorum's leadership, before returning to Naboo, where she successfully led a revolt against the occupation of the Trade Federation. During this battle, Qui-Gon's mysterious attacker reappeared, and successfully murdered him, though the attacker in turn was defeated by Obi-Wan Kenobi. It became obvious to Yoda and others on the Council that the Sith had indeed returned; however, it was not clear whether the attacker Kenobi "killed" was the Sith Master or apprentice.[[21]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace-21)

 [![Yoda with Kenobi and Skywalker during the mission to Mawan](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Anakin_The_Shadow_Trap2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20061215203325) [![Yoda with Kenobi and Skywalker during the mission to Mawan](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Anakin_The_Shadow_Trap2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20061215203325)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/Anakin_The_Shadow_Trap2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20061215203325) 

Yoda with Kenobi and Skywalker during the mission to Mawan

 

Following Amidala's call for a vote of no confidence in Valorum's leadership of the Senate, Naboo's own [senator](/wiki/Senator/Legends "Senator/Legends"), [Palpatine](/wiki/Palpatine/Legends "Palpatine/Legends"), was elected the new Supreme Chancellor of the Galactic Republic. In addition, the Council against Yoda's wishes, granted Obi-Wan, now a Jedi Knight, permission to train Anakin Skywalker as a Jedi. He vocally expressed his disapproval of the Council's decision, but reluctantly relented when he learned that Obi-Wan was willing to even go against the decision of the Council if it meant fulfilling Qui-Gon's final wish.[[21]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_I:_The_Phantom_Menace-21)

In circa [31 BBY](/wiki/31_BBY/Legends "31 BBY/Legends"), the Human [Len Markus](/wiki/Len_Markus "Len Markus") seized the [Darkstaff](/wiki/Darkstaff "Darkstaff"), an ancient [dark side artifact](/wiki/Dark_side_artifact/Legends "Dark side artifact/Legends"), from the [Cularin asteroid belt](/wiki/Cularin_asteroid_belt "Cularin asteroid belt"), causing the [Cularin system](/wiki/Cularin_system/Legends "Cularin system/Legends") to [disappear](/wiki/Cularin%27s_disappearance "Cularin's disappearance") from [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy/Legends "The galaxy/Legends") for ten years. The event caused a surge of dark-side energy, which was so strong that it almost hospitalized Yoda. However, despite the physical absence of the system, Yoda could sense that the star system's inhabitants were still alive.[[23]](#cite_note-Philology-23)

### Mission to Mawan ([25 BBY](/wiki/26_BBY/Legends "26 BBY/Legends"))[]

Seven years after the events at Naboo, Yoda went on a negotiation mission to [Mawan](/wiki/Mawan/Legends "Mawan/Legends") with Obi-Wan, Anakin and Yaddle. Their goal was to settle a devastating civil war between three crime gangs. These gangs, led by [Decca the Hutt](/wiki/Decca_Besadii_Diori "Decca Besadii Diori"), [Feeana Tala](/wiki/Feeana_Tala "Feeana Tala"), and [Striker](/wiki/Granta_Omega "Granta Omega"), caused the remainder of the population to take refuge underground. Unbeknownst to them, the chaotic planet was a trap set for the Jedi by Striker, whose true identity was [Granta Omega](/wiki/Granta_Omega "Granta Omega"), son of [Xanatos](/wiki/Xanatos "Xanatos"). After kidnapping Anakin, he released a deadly chemical weapon that Yaddle intercepted, killing her when she absorbed it through the Force. However, through her sacrifice, she saved the city of Naatan. The weapon was intended by its vengeful maker to kill thousands if he was betrayed by any opposition, and as his insurance to escape offworld, but it failed because of what Yaddle had done. Anakin and Obi-Wan managed to bring peace to Mawan, but Anakin still felt responsible for the death of the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council/Legends "Jedi High Council/Legends") member. Yoda, despite the loss of Yaddle, still managed to convince Decca to evacuate with her illegal operations by "suggesting" that the Jedi Council might build a Temple on the planet, which was more than enough to make the criminal flee.[[24]](#cite_note-Jedi_Quest:_The_Shadow_Trap-24)

### Separatist Crisis ([24 BBY](/wiki/24_BBY/Legends "24 BBY/Legends")–[22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY/Legends "22 BBY/Legends"))[]

:   "*Master Yoda, do you think it will really come to war?"   
     "Hmmm. The dark side clouds everything. Impossible to see, the future is.*"
:   ―Palpatine and Yoda[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

Spurred by the failure of the Senate to even vote on the [Financial Reform Act](/wiki/Financial_Reform_Act "Financial Reform Act"), many planets, systems and corporations began to withdraw from the Republic. In addition, and particularly troubling for the Jedi, especially Yoda, the disillusioned former Jedi Count Dooku, who had once studied under Yoda, was the leading voice among these Separatists.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

#### Attempts on Senator Amidala[]

 [![Yoda and other members of the Council advise the Chancellor during the Separatist Crisis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Chancellors_Office.png/revision/latest?cb=20161015185023) [![Yoda and other members of the Council advise the Chancellor during the Separatist Crisis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Chancellors_Office.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20161015185023)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Chancellors_Office.png/revision/latest?cb=20161015185023) 

Yoda and other members of the Council advise the Chancellor during the Separatist Crisis.

 

The growing threat prompted members of the Senate to call for a [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act/Legends "Military Creation Act/Legends"), which would allow Supreme Chancellor Palpatine to create an army for the Republic. The leader of the opposition against this act was Senator Padmé Amidala, the former Queen of Naboo. When the time to vote on the act arrived, and Amidala arrived on Coruscant, an attempt was made upon her life, though she survived.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

The Jedi Council, disturbed by this, had Jedi Knight Obi-Wan Kenobi and his apprentice, Anakin Skywalker, placed in charge of the Senator's safety. Following a second attempt on the life of Amidala, Kenobi and Skywalker captured the bounty hunter responsible, only to have her killed by a second bounty hunter, through the use of a toxic dart, during her interrogation.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

The Council had Kenobi trace the second bounty hunter, while Skywalker was to accompany Amidala to the safety of her homeworld. Yoda helped Kenobi solve the mystery behind the missing planet [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino/Legends "Kamino/Legends"), where the Jedi Knight had traced the origins of the toxic dart; it was Yoda's belief that certain files had been deleted from the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives/Legends "Jedi Archives/Legends") for an unknown purpose. Even more disturbing, only a Jedi would have been capable of erasing the files.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

#### Clone army[]

:   "*Blind we are, if creation of this clone army, we could not see.*"  
    "*I think it is time we informed the Senate that our ability to use the Force has diminished.*"  
    "*Only the Dark Lords of the Sith know of our weakness. If informed, the Senate is, multiply, our adversaries will.*"
:   ―Yoda and Mace Windu[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

Upon making his way to Kamino, Obi-Wan Kenobi discovered that a massive [army of clones](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic/Legends "Grand Army of the Republic/Legends") was being created, apparently on the orders of the late Jedi Master [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas/Legends "Sifo-Dyas/Legends"). Kenobi reported this to Masters Mace Windu and Yoda, the senior members of the Council, who had had no knowledge of a clone army. Obi-Wan felt certain that the template of the clone army, a bounty hunter named [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett/Legends "Jango Fett/Legends"), was the same bounty hunter who had been involved in the attempts on Senator Amidala's life.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

While waiting for Kenobi's report, Yoda meditated. He heard the voice of the spirit of Qui-Gon Jinn and sensed that [something](/wiki/Mission_to_rescue_Shmi_Skywalker_Lars/Legends "Mission to rescue Shmi Skywalker Lars/Legends") had happened to Anakin Skywalker. He conferred with Windu that the young Padawan was in "pain. *Terrible* pain."[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

Kenobi traced Fett to [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis/Legends "Geonosis/Legends"), only to be captured during his report, which detailed his discovery that Count Dooku had formed an alliance of powerful corporations into a [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems/Legends "Confederacy of Independent Systems/Legends"). This caused the Senate to grant the Chancellor emergency powers, with which he authorized the Grand Army of the Republic while Senator Amidala and Anakin Skywalker attempted to rescue Kenobi, only to be captured themselves. In response, Master Windu formed a strike team to extract the captured trio, while Yoda went to Kamino in an attempt to discover the truth of the clone army, and also to bring some of those troops to Geonosis.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

### Clone Wars ([22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY/Legends "22 BBY/Legends")–[19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY/Legends "19 BBY/Legends"))[]

#### Battle of Geonosis[]

:   "*The shroud of the dark side has fallen. Begun, the Clone War has.*"
:   ―Master Yoda[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

 [![Yoda battles his former ,  , on .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Yoda1280.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070224213010) [![Yoda battles his former ,  , on .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Yoda1280.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20070224213010)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/Yoda1280.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070224213010) 

Yoda battles his former [student](/wiki/Padawan/Legends "Padawan/Legends"), [Count](/wiki/Count/Legends "Count/Legends") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku/Legends "Dooku/Legends"), on [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis/Legends "Geonosis/Legends").

 

Windu and the Jedi were confronted by a huge droid army under the command of Count Dooku, with only a handful surviving, when, with the rank of General, Yoda arrived with a contingent of the new clone army. Yoda commanded the forces of the Republic, before feeling a disturbance in the Force.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

Master Yoda arrived in a hangar to confront Dooku, after he had grievously wounded Skywalker and Kenobi. After deflecting Dooku's Force powers, among which was [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning/Legends "Force lightning/Legends"), Yoda realized that Dooku had turned to the dark side of the Force, becoming a [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord/Legends "Sith Lord/Legends"). A lightsaber duel began between the two, with Dooku faring well against his old master. Yet, as the duel progressed the Grand Master of the Jedi showed speed and agility so incredible that it began to overwhelm Dooku, plus he was the only one save for one other being in the galaxy that held skill enough with a blade equal or even greater than the Makashi master. Yoda almost defeated Dooku, but the Sith Lord used the Force to drop a pillar over Obi-Wan and Anakin. While Yoda concentrated on stopping the massive construction from crushing the two Jedi, Dooku made his escape.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)

Though the Republic won the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis/Legends "First Battle of Geonosis/Legends") under the direction of Yoda, many Jedi were killed. More importantly, the thousand-year peace that had existed since the [Seventh Battle of Ruusan](/wiki/Seventh_Battle_of_Ruusan "Seventh Battle of Ruusan") had ended. Yoda sensed that the Clone Wars would be a long and tumultuous period for both the Republic and the Jedi Order, and indeed they were, shaking the galaxy to its very core. During the Clone Wars, Yoda, along with many other Jedi Masters, was forced to become a general fighting in various battles for the Republic on worlds across the galaxy.[[26]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Clone_Wars-26)

#### Frontline warrior[]

:   "*Darker, the coming storm grows. I fear the dark cloud of the Sith shrouds us all.*"
:   ―Yoda — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e3/DarkerTheComingStormGrows-CW20.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250320002731)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:DarkerTheComingStormGrows-CW20.flac "File:DarkerTheComingStormGrows-CW20.flac"))[[27]](#cite_note-CW20-27)

 [![Yoda during the ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Kybuckcharge_cw1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090912035739) [![Yoda during the ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Kybuckcharge_cw1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20090912035739)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Kybuckcharge_cw1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090912035739) 

Yoda during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars/Legends "Clone Wars/Legends")

 

Shortly after the beginning of the war, Yoda took the title of [Master of the Order](/wiki/Master_of_the_Order/Legends "Master of the Order/Legends") from Mace Windu. Early in the conflict, Yoda saw front-line action at the [Battle of Axion](/wiki/Battle_of_Axion "Battle of Axion"), leading [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper/Legends "Clone trooper/Legends") into battle atop [his](/wiki/Yoda%27s_kybuck "Yoda's kybuck") [kybuck](/wiki/Kybuck/Legends "Kybuck/Legends") steed. On that contested world, he saved the life of [Commander](/wiki/Commander/Legends "Commander/Legends") [Brolis](/wiki/Brolis "Brolis"), and in the process defeated a [Hailfire droid](/wiki/IG-227_Hailfire-class_droid_tank/Legends "IG-227 Hailfire-class droid tank/Legends") in single combat.[[28]](#cite_note-duel-28) Around the time of the [Battle of Muunilinst](/wiki/Battle_of_Muunilinst/Legends "Battle of Muunilinst/Legends"), Yoda came to the rescue of Jedi, [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli/Legends "Luminara Unduli/Legends") and [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee/Legends "Barriss Offee/Legends"), with the help of Senator Padmé Amidala of Naboo after the [Crystal Caves](/wiki/Crystal_Cave/Legends "Crystal Cave/Legends") on [Ilum](/wiki/Ilum/Legends "Ilum/Legends") were destroyed by [chameleon droids](/wiki/Spelunker_probe_droid/Legends "Spelunker probe droid/Legends"). Yoda sensed Unduli and Offee's peril through the Force, and during his rescue mission destroyed dozens of chameleon droids, before rescuing the pair. On Ilum, Yoda learned that Dooku's treachery ran deeper than he had believed, for the former Jedi Master had ordered the attack on the crystal temple.[[26]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Clone_Wars-26)

 [![Yoda mourns 's death](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/28/AlaricDeath.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150720052454) [![Yoda mourns 's death](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/28/AlaricDeath.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20150720052454)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/28/AlaricDeath.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150720052454) 

Yoda mourns [Alaric](/wiki/Alaric_(Sephi) "Alaric (Sephi)")'s death

 

Yoda had lost his former Padawan to the dark side before the war began, but during the conflict, Yoda lost another good friend. [King](/wiki/King/Legends "King/Legends") [Alaric](/wiki/Alaric_(Sephi) "Alaric (Sephi)") of [Thustra](/wiki/Thustra/Legends "Thustra/Legends") was planning to secede his homeworld to the Confederacy of Independent Systems, although he intended to rejoin the Republic when the corruption he had witnessed was gone. Yoda traveled to Thustra to speak with Alaric, but his old friend was resolute, and eventually, his world became embroiled in battle. Unwilling to face the state of his world, Alaric drew a [blaster](/wiki/Blaster/Legends "Blaster/Legends") on Yoda, knowing his friend would be forced to defend himself. Left with no choice, Yoda deflected the bolt into the body of the King. Yoda lamented the fall of his friend, but more worrying was how even he had been forced to draw his blade in battle, and feared he would have to draw it again in many battles to come.[[29]](#cite_note-JediYoda-29)

The Jedi Grand Master oversaw many missions from the Jedi Temple as well, sifting through several intelligence reports and working with the Council to determine which to act upon. He learned through Obi-Wan Kenobi that [Dexter Jettster](/wiki/Dexter_Jettster/Legends "Dexter Jettster/Legends") was a reliable informant, and soon learned to place his trust in [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa/Legends "Bail Prestor Organa/Legends") as well after the senator revealed information of a hitherto unknown Sith planet designated [Zigoola](/wiki/Zigoola "Zigoola"). Kenobi and Organa soon departed to bring an end to the planet, and Yoda and Mace Windu meditated and lent their support from afar, sensing the completion of their mission upon its closure and calling upon Padmé Amidala once more to go and retrieve them.[[30]](#cite_note-Wild_Space-30)

When the Republic was contacted by crime lord [Jabba](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure/Legends "Jabba Desilijic Tiure/Legends") the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt/Legends "Hutt/Legends"), in regards to his missing son, [Rotta](/wiki/Rotta/Legends "Rotta/Legends"), and offered the Republic use of Hutt hyperspace lanes, should the Republic rescue the missing Huttlet, it became apparent that the only Jedi the Order could spare for the mission were Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker. However, the two were embroiled in an ongoing [conflict](/wiki/Battle_of_Christophsis/Legends "Battle of Christophsis/Legends") on [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis/Legends "Christophsis/Legends"), and communications were impossible. As such, Yoda sent a youngling, [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano/Legends "Ahsoka Tano/Legends"), to inform the pair of their new mission, and in addition, assigned her as Skywalker's Padawan. The trio eventually succeeded in rescuing Jabba's son, allowing the Republic to use unknown Hutt hyperspace lanes, an advantage the Confederacy did not have.[[31]](#cite_note-CloneWarsMovie-31)

#### Rugosa[]

:   **Ventress**: "*If Yoda is indeed the Jedi warrior you believe he is, let him prove it. Allow me to send my best troops to capture him. If he escapes, join the Republic. But should my droids defeat Yoda, consider an alliance with the Separatists.*"
:   **Katuunko**: "*I did not request Yoda's presence here to test him in battle.*"
:   **Yoda**: "*Accept the challenge I do, Your Highness. Arrive by nightfall, I* will*.*"
:   ―Asajj Ventress places the terms of the competition; Yoda accepts — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/YodaAcceptsChallenge.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250329120901)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:YodaAcceptsChallenge.flac "File:YodaAcceptsChallenge.flac"))[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32)

 [![Yoda during the mission to Rugosa](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/Yoda_Ambush.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090922180136) [![Yoda during the mission to Rugosa](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/Yoda_Ambush.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20090922180136)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/Yoda_Ambush.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090922180136) 

Yoda during the mission to Rugosa

 

Shortly after, Yoda was selected to lead diplomatic relations with the [Toydarian](/wiki/Toydarian/Legends "Toydarian/Legends") King [Katuunko](/wiki/Katuunko/Legends "Katuunko/Legends"), as the Republic wished to build a base in his system to further combat the Confederacy in the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories/Legends "Outer Rim Territories/Legends"). However, the Confederacy intercepted communications between the king and the Republic with the newly built [Skytop Station](/wiki/Skytop_Station/Legends "Skytop Station/Legends"), and, hoping to derail the negotiations, Separatist leader Count Dooku sent his apprentice [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress/Legends "Asajj Ventress/Legends") to the neutral moon of [Rugosa](/wiki/Rugosa/Legends "Rugosa/Legends"), where the negotiations were scheduled to take place. When Master Yoda's warship arrived at Rugosa, it was immediately set upon by several Separatist cruisers; however, Yoda refused to be deterred, and escaped the frenzy via [escape pod](/wiki/Escape_pod/Legends "Escape pod/Legends") along with three clone troopers, and landed safely on the moon's surface.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32)

Once on the moon, the Jedi Grand Master contacted Katuunko, and after becoming aware of Ventress's presence, agreed to a wager: should Yoda defeat Ventress' best troops, Toydaria would join the Republic; however, should Ventress's forces overwhelm Yoda, then the king would ally his system with the Confederacy. Katuunko insisted that the Dark Jedi ensure Yoda be given a fair fight, to which she agreed. After returning to her base, Ventress contacted Dooku and stated that her forces were being deployed. She did not intend for Yoda to get his fair fight and dispatched the recently promoted [224](/wiki/224/Legends "224/Legends") with the task of leading the droid forces, and the battle droids prepared to ambush the Republic's diplomatic squad. Led by 224 in his [Armored Assault Tank](/wiki/Armored_Assault_Tank/Legends "Armored Assault Tank/Legends"), the main column of Confederate forces advanced into the jungle. Yoda and his men made their way to the rendezvous position on a different path, as the Jedi Master was certain that their enemies were already heading toward them. The droids began to go through the [coral](/wiki/Rugosa_land_coral "Rugosa land coral") of the jungle, but the dense foliage prevented the [tanks](/wiki/Tank/Legends "Tank/Legends") from advancing.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32)

 [![Yoda eliminates a Confederate tank.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/Yoda_the_great_warrior.png/revision/latest?cb=20120916032109) [![Yoda eliminates a Confederate tank.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/Yoda_the_great_warrior.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20120916032109)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/Yoda_the_great_warrior.png/revision/latest?cb=20120916032109) 

Yoda eliminates a Confederate tank.

 

Yoda and the clones split up, seeking to use their surroundings to their advantage.[[33]](#cite_note-Ambush_Decoded-33) The clones engaged a squad of B1 battle droids from the south and managed to defeat them, but [B2 super battle droids](/wiki/B2-series_super_battle_droid/Legends "B2-series super battle droid/Legends") then came to attack the clones, and the three were forced to flee. Yoda, meanwhile, was able to defeat an entire squad of droids on his own without even using his [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber/Legends "Lightsaber/Legends"). [CC-4477](/wiki/Thire/Legends "Thire/Legends") was hit by a [rocket](/wiki/Missile/Legends "Missile/Legends") fired by a [B2-HA series super battle droid](/wiki/B2-HA_super_battle_droid/Legends "B2-HA super battle droid/Legends") and was wounded in the leg. Yoda appeared and aided the clones, using the Force to [turn around](/wiki/Telekinesis/Legends "Telekinesis/Legends") a battle droid and destroy the rest of the squad. [Droidekas](/wiki/Droideka/Legends "Droideka/Legends") soon appeared, and the Republic forces fled. Yoda, clinging onto CC-4477's back, deflected the [lasers](/wiki/Laser/Legends "Laser/Legends") at a nearby tall formation of land coral, causing the droids to be squashed and the four escaped to a cave to rest. The clones learned that they were low on ammunition, but the Jedi Master imparted his wisdom on the clone troopers to further inspire their efforts.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32)

After hearing the sounds of the droids approaching in the distance, Yoda and the clones exited the cave. The Jedi and his men arrived on a ridge to observe the advancing droids below, which were passing through a narrow pathway. Yoda left the clones on the ridge and faced three tanks and a large number of droids alone. The Jedi Master destroyed all of them, along with 224, leaving Katuunko amused and Ventress angry. However, Ventress did not give up easily; the Dark Acolyte broke the terms of the competition and secretly sent several droidekas to deal with the Jedi Master. As Yoda destroyed the last Confederate tank, the droidekas arrived, and the Jedi Master began blocking their laser attacks. CC-4477 launched the last of the rockets at an overhanging rock above the canyon, causing an avalanche to crush the droids. Yoda then led the clones to the rendezvous point, remarking that it was not polite to be late.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32)

Katuunko was greatly amused by the droids' defeat. Through a holotransmission, the king informed Dooku that one Jedi was not worth a hundred battle droids, but rather a thousand, and stated that he would be joining the Republic. The count urged him to reconsider, but the Toydarian king refused to deal with those who went back on their promises, as Ventress had broken the terms of the competition. Seeing that his plan had failed, Dooku ordered Ventress to kill the king, believing that negotiations might go smoother with his successor. Katuunko's guards tried to stop the Dark Acolyte, but Ventress merely Force-pushed them aside, knocking them unconscious. As Ventress attacked the king with her [paired lightsabers](/wiki/Interlocking_hilt "Interlocking hilt"), she was confronted by Yoda, having arrived in time to save the king.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32)

 [![Ventress' assassination attempt is thwarted by Master Yoda.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/Ventress_strikes.png/revision/latest?cb=20120916031919) [![Ventress' assassination attempt is thwarted by Master Yoda.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/Ventress_strikes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20120916031919)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/Ventress_strikes.png/revision/latest?cb=20120916031919) 

Ventress' assassination attempt is thwarted by Master Yoda.

 

Yoda used the Force to stop the Dark Acolyte's [death](/wiki/Death/Legends "Death/Legends") blow from being struck. As Ventress' droid escorts were dispatched by the clones, Yoda [disarmed](/wiki/Telekinesis/Legends#Force_Disarm "Telekinesis/Legends") Ventress herself, and after examining her lightsabers, the Jedi returned them to her,[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32) having proven they were useless against his telekinesis,[[33]](#cite_note-Ambush_Decoded-33) while commenting that she still had much to learn. Ventress was outnumbered, and Yoda suggested that she surrender. In order to escape, Ventress detonated pre-planted explosives and caused the hillside adjacent to the Republic forces to collapse. Yoda was forced to telekinetically stop the rocks from crushing all of them, and as he did so, Ventress seized the opportunity and fled to [her ship](/wiki/Punworcca_116-class_interstellar_sloop/Legends "Punworcca 116-class interstellar sloop/Legends"). Dooku, watching the events unfold through the holoprojector, commented before taking his leave that it was a pity that he had not been there himself.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32)

With the Confederate threat over, Yoda was able to enter into negotiations with Katuunko. The king stated that discussions were unnecessary, however, as the Jedi had already proven his worth.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32) Katuunko presented his [ceremonial sword](/wiki/Ceremonial_sword/Legends "Ceremonial sword/Legends") to Yoda and entrusted him with his planet's protection[[33]](#cite_note-Ambush_Decoded-33) while pledging Toydaria's support to the Republic, declaring that it would be an honor to fight on their side.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32)

#### The *Malevolence*[]

After the appearance of a [mysterious Separatist super weapon](/wiki/Malevolence/Legends "Malevolence/Legends") that had ambushed several Republic fleets and left no survivors, Yoda and the Council sent one among its number, Jedi Master Plo Koon, to track down the unknown threat. After Master Koon discovered the weapon, he contacted the Jedi general in the closest system to him, Anakin Skywalker. However, during the transmission, Koon's communication systems were jammed, and the Republic lost contact with his fleet. Masters Yoda, Windu and Kenobi, in conjunction with Supreme Chancellor Palpatine, agreed that sending a task force to search for survivors of the latest attack would prove risky; however, Skywalker disobeyed their orders, and through his Padawan Ahsoka Tano's unique connection through the Force to Master Koon, rescued the stranded Jedi Master and his few remaining troops. With Master Koon alive to report on the nature of the Separatist weapon, the Republic learned that the Separatists had acquired giant [ion cannons](/wiki/Ion_cannon/Legends "Ion cannon/Legends") capable of disabling any fleet.[[34]](#cite_note-Rising_Malevolence-34)

 [![Yoda](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/Yoda_CN.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091112143745) [![Yoda](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/Yoda_CN.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091112143745)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9d/Yoda_CN.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091112143745) 

Yoda

 

A plan devised and instigated by Skywalker proved able to destroy the *Malevolence*'s primary weapon, and later, during a mission to rescue the captive Senator Amidala of Naboo, the giant warship was rigged to pilot itself into a nearby moon, destroying it, and freeing the Republic from the danger it represented.[[35]](#cite_note-DM-35)

#### Gunray's capture[]

A short time later, Senator Amidala captured important Separatist leader [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray/Legends "Nute Gunray/Legends") on [Rodia](/wiki/Rodia/Legends "Rodia/Legends"). As such, the Council sent Jedi Master Luminara Unduli and Padawan Ahsoka Tano to escort the viceroy to Coruscant, where he would face trial for war crimes. While guarding the viceroy, Master Unduli was to interrogate him, in the hopes of learning important Separatist secrets.[[36]](#cite_note-CoD-36)

However, Unduli's starship came under Separatist assault and was boarded by large numbers of droids. Though Unduli defeated the droids, she was unprepared for the far greater adversary that had infiltrated the ship: Asajj Ventress. Ventress dueled both Unduli and Tano, holding them off while her secret ally, the Senate Commando [Faro Argyus](/wiki/Faro_Argyus/Legends "Faro Argyus/Legends"), betrayed his fellows and rescued Gunray. After receiving word of this, Ventress escaped the Jedi, who were left to explain the catastrophe to Master Yoda.[[36]](#cite_note-CoD-36)

 [![Fisto reports to Windu and Yoda.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Council_report.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924013733) [![Fisto reports to Windu and Yoda.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Council_report.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20120924013733)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/66/Council_report.png/revision/latest?cb=20120924013733) 

Fisto reports to Windu and Yoda.

 

Yoda was particularly disturbed by the betrayal of Argyus, as he felt it revealed that the Republic's enemies were everywhere. However, he supported Master Unduli's proposal that Master [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto/Legends "Kit Fisto/Legends") move to recapture Gunray, his escape ship having been tracked, as the [Nautolan's](/wiki/Nautolan/Legends "Nautolan/Legends") fleet was nearer the viceroy's last known position.[[36]](#cite_note-CoD-36)

Fisto was largely led on a wild bantha chase, however. Rather than recapturing Gunray, the Nautolan was forced to duel General Grievous and to watch his former Padawan, [Nahdar Vebb](/wiki/Nahdar_Vebb/Legends "Nahdar Vebb/Legends"), die at the cyborg's hands. After he escaped, Fisto reported to the Council in the persons of Mace Windu and Yoda. Yoda lamented that Vebb's death was largely the result of his own hubris and feared that in the war there was a danger of the Jedi losing the very essence of who they were.[[37]](#cite_note-LoG-37)

#### Dealing with pirates[]

Skywalker and Kenobi later launched a mission to capture the heart of the Confederacy, Count Dooku, though they were unsuccessful. However, where Skywalker and Kenobi failed, lowly pirates succeeded and contacted the Chancellor's office demanding a reward in return for the Sith Lord. Yoda confirmed that the lightsaber handled by the head of the pirate organization, [Hondo Ohnaka](/wiki/Hondo_Ohnaka/Legends "Hondo Ohnaka/Legends"), was indeed his former apprentice's.[[38]](#cite_note-DC-38)

Under the advice of Senator Amidala, the Council sent Kenobi and Skywalker to confirm Dooku's capture, which they ultimately did. However, Ohnaka had them captured in addition to Dooku, in the hopes of garnering a further reward from the Republic. Though Skywalker and Kenobi ultimately escaped with the help of the Republic dignitaries sent to deliver the reward, it came at the expense of the respected Senator [Kharrus](/wiki/Kharrus/Legends "Kharrus/Legends")' life, while Dooku managed to escape capture.[[39]](#cite_note-TGG-39)

#### Blue Shadow Virus[]

 [![Yoda and Windu conferring with the Naboo](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Naboo_holo_conference.png/revision/latest?cb=20121002021957) [![Yoda and Windu conferring with the Naboo](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Naboo_holo_conference.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20121002021957)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/90/Naboo_holo_conference.png/revision/latest?cb=20121002021957) 

Yoda and Windu conferring with the Naboo

 

Later, the Naboo contacted the Council and asked Masters Windu and Yoda to send two Jedi, specifically Kenobi and Skywalker due to their relations with the native Gungans, to help uncover a Separatist bio-lab believed to have been established on world. While the Jedi did discover the lab and prepare its resident scientist Dr. [Nuvo Vindi](/wiki/Nuvo_Vindi/Legends "Nuvo Vindi/Legends") for trial, a deadly virus he had prepared, the [Blue Shadow Virus](/wiki/Blue_Shadow_Virus/Legends "Blue Shadow Virus/Legends"), was released, infecting Senator Amidala and Ahsoka Tano. They were administered the rare antidote before the virus could claim them.[[40]](#cite_note-BSV-40)[[41]](#cite_note-MoaTM-41)

#### Ryloth[]

Later, when Master Windu led an assault on the planet Ryloth aimed at freeing the Twi'leki population from Separatist occupation, Yoda remained on Coruscant. However, the diminutive Jedi Master acted as advisor to Windu and was involved in tactical discussions regarding how to capture the capital city of [Lessu](/wiki/Lessu_City/Legends "Lessu City/Legends"). Yoda counseled Windu that it was important that the Separatist leader [Wat Tambor](/wiki/Wat_Tambor/Legends "Wat Tambor/Legends"), who was responsible for the occupation of Ryloth, be captured to answer for his many war crimes. Ultimately, Windu agreed with Master Yoda and was able to capture the Separatist Council member at the conclusion of the [Battle of Ryloth](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth/Legends "Battle of Ryloth/Legends").[[42]](#cite_note-LoR-42)

#### Stolen holocron[]

:   "*Master Yoda, what is it?*"  
    "*A disturbance in the Force. Intruders there will be, in this Temple.*"
:   ―[Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight/Legends "Jedi Knight/Legends") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker/Legends "Anakin Skywalker/Legends") and [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master/Legends "Grand Master/Legends") Yoda[[43]](#cite_note-HH-43)

Following the [First Battle of Felucia](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Felucia/Legends "First Battle of Felucia/Legends"), Master Yoda presided over a meeting of the Jedi Council which heard that Padawan Ahsoka Tano had refused to comply with orders given to her by her superior Jedi Master Obi-Wan Kenobi. In punishment for her actions, Ahsoka was appointed as a guard of the Jedi Archives in order to spend time away from the battlefield.[[43]](#cite_note-HH-43)

Later, while discussing the impact the defeat at Felucia would have on Republic war efforts in the region with Master Kenobi and Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker, Yoda was overcome by a disturbance in the Force which revealed to him that intruders planned to infiltrate the Jedi Temple. Kenobi and Skywalker incorrectly deduced that the culprits would attempt to steal the Jedi Order's transmission codes, and as such, focused their efforts on securing the codes. Yoda later sensed the arrival of the intruders and suggested to Kenobi and Skywalker that their enemies may head to the [Jedi Temple communication center](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_communication_center/Legends "Jedi Temple communication center/Legends"). The Grand Master then met there with Masters Mace Windu, Kit Fisto and [Aayla Secura](/wiki/Aayla_Secura/Legends "Aayla Secura/Legends") after having placed the Temple on high alert.[[43]](#cite_note-HH-43)

 [![Master Yoda stands at the entrance to the Holocron Chamber.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/YodaHolocronChamber-HH.png/revision/latest?cb=20120827221907) [![Master Yoda stands at the entrance to the Holocron Chamber.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/YodaHolocronChamber-HH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20120827221907)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/be/YodaHolocronChamber-HH.png/revision/latest?cb=20120827221907) 

Master Yoda stands at the entrance to the Holocron Chamber.

 

As Kenobi and Skywalker tracked the intruders through the Temple's ventilation system, Master Yoda deduced that it was likely that the intruders were receiving assistance from within the Temple considering their ability to avoid the two Jedi trailing them. As such, the diminutive Master contacted Ahsoka Tano and cautioned her that he sensed deception and that there was somebody in the Archives impersonating a Jedi. Fortunately, Tano was able to subdue the impostor, a [Clawdite](/wiki/Clawdite/Legends "Clawdite/Legends") [changeling](/wiki/Changeling/Legends "Changeling/Legends") named [Cato Parasitti](/wiki/Cato_Parasitti/Legends "Cato Parasitti/Legends"), who had been impersonating Master [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu/Legends "Jocasta Nu/Legends") and feeding her employer [Cad Bane](/wiki/Cad_Bane/Legends "Cad Bane/Legends") information from the Jedi Archives.[[43]](#cite_note-HH-43)

Nonetheless, Bane's scheme worked, as he was able to keep the Jedi off his tail long enough to break into the [Holocron Chamber](/wiki/Holocron_Chamber "Holocron Chamber") and steal a Jedi holocron as ordered by the Sith Lord Darth Sidious. However, Parasitti revealed to the Jedi that Bane's next target was Jedi Master [Bolla Ropal](/wiki/Bolla_Ropal/Legends "Bolla Ropal/Legends"). This allowed the Jedi to deduce that Bane was after the [Kyber memory crystal](/wiki/Kyber_memory_crystal/Legends "Kyber memory crystal/Legends") in Ropal's keeping, which when combined with a holocron would reveal a list of all known Force-sensitive children in the galaxy.[[43]](#cite_note-HH-43)

While Skywalker and Tano were dispatched to protect Master Ropal, they were ultimately too late; Ropal was captured and died under torture, refusing to use the Force to help Bane unite the holocron and Kyber crystal. However, the Jedi believed that Bane himself was killed during the [Battle of Devaron](/wiki/Battle_of_Devaron/Legends "Battle of Devaron/Legends"), though he later proved to have survived. Prior to faking his death, Bane was able to coerce Skywalker into uniting the holocron and memory crystal, and as such, the bounty hunter began collecting the Force-sensitive children on behalf of Sidious.[[44]](#cite_note-CargoofDoom-44)

Later, Yoda led Windu, Kenobi and Skywalker in using the Force to pinpoint which children would be targeted by Bane. Yoda sensed that a child on Rodia was in danger, as well as one on Naboo. However, when Master Windu asserted that a child from [Glee Anselm](/wiki/Glee_Anselm/Legends "Glee Anselm/Legends") was being targeted by Bane, Yoda revealed that the infant had already been claimed by the bounty hunter and that the dark side hid his fate. Kenobi proved unable to prevent Bane from capturing the Rodian, but Skywalker and his Padawan captured Bane when he ventured to Naboo.[[44]](#cite_note-CargoofDoom-44)

Masters Kenobi and Windu then used Bane to relocate the stolen holocron, though the bounty hunter escaped in the process. However, even without Bane, Skywalker and his Padawan discovered a secret facility on [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar/Legends "Mustafar/Legends") where the captured children were hidden, and ultimately rescued them.[[44]](#cite_note-CargoofDoom-44)

#### The Zillo Beast[]

 [![Yoda, Aayla Secura, and Anakin Skywalker fend off the toxin-bombs.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/ForceBarrier-ZBSB.png/revision/latest?cb=20120912220529) [![Yoda, Aayla Secura, and Anakin Skywalker fend off the toxin-bombs.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/ForceBarrier-ZBSB.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20120912220529)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/ForceBarrier-ZBSB.png/revision/latest?cb=20120912220529) 

Yoda, Aayla Secura, and Anakin Skywalker fend off the toxin-bombs.

 

When Supreme Chancellor Palpatine discovered the [Zillo Beast](/wiki/Zillo_Beast/Legends "Zillo Beast/Legends") on [Malastare](/wiki/Malastare/Legends "Malastare/Legends") and ordered it brought to Coruscant for research, it promptly escaped and made a beeline for the Senate building, necessitating the interference of Yoda and the Jedi Order. Dismissing Mace Windu's suggestion to shoot the beast down with stun rays, Yoda and Aayla Secura clambered atop the beast's back, distracting it with their lightsabers to buy Republic forces time to rescue the shuttle in the creature's grasp with Palpatine, Anakin Skywalker, and Padmé Amidala inside. When all the shuttle's occupants were brought to safety, Yoda aided Secura and Skywalker in protecting the group from the toxin-bombs detonated to kill the beast.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-45)

#### Savage Opress[]

:   "*A creature from the same species he is. From Dathomir.*"
:   ―Yoda assures Obi-Wan Kenobi that Savage Opress is not Darth Maul.[[46]](#cite_note-Witches-46)

Yoda and Mace Windu later showed Obi-Wan Kenobi footage of a recent [massacre](/wiki/Devaron_massacre/Legends "Devaron massacre/Legends") on [Devaron](/wiki/Devaron/Legends "Devaron/Legends"), in which Jedi Master [Halsey](/wiki/Halsey/Legends "Halsey/Legends") and his Padawan [Knox](/wiki/Knox/Legends "Knox/Legends") were brutally murdered by an [unknown assassin](/wiki/Savage_Opress/Legends "Savage Opress/Legends"). The footage baffled Kenobi, for he believed he had killed the Sith Lord Darth Maul, but Yoda pointed out that it was a creature of the same species from Dathomir. Yoda tasked Kenobi with going to Dathomir to find this threat and defeat it.[[47]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-47)

#### Mortis communication[]

The Jedi Council later received a mysterious transmission which was over two thousand years old. After the Council reviewed the ancient transmission, they dispatched Obi-Wan Kenobi, Anakin Skywalker and Ahsoka Tano to uncover if it was a Separatist trap. As a precaution, they sent a heavily armed fleet to accompany them.

When the trio returned, Yoda learned from Kenobi that they encountered three beings: the [Father](/wiki/Father_(Mortis)/Legends "Father (Mortis)/Legends"), [Son](/wiki/Son/Legends "Son/Legends") and [Daughter](/wiki/Daughter/Legends "Daughter/Legends"), who resembled the [light](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force/Legends "Light side of the Force/Legends") and dark sides of the Force.

#### Rescue of Even Piell[]

Jedi Master and councilor [Even Piell](/wiki/Even_Piell/Legends "Even Piell/Legends") was taken [prisoner](/wiki/Capture_of_Even_Piell/Legends "Capture of Even Piell/Legends") by Separatist forces after he recovered the [Nexus Route](/wiki/Nexus_Route/Legends "Nexus Route/Legends") coordinates, which were crucial to the war effort. As a result, the Jedi Council set up a [rescue attempt](/wiki/Battle_of_Lola_Sayu/Legends "Battle of Lola Sayu/Legends"), with Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker in charge. Ahsoka Tano also went along, disobeying orders to stay.

But the rescue attempt failed, and the team split up and later rejoined after their ship was destroyed. Yoda, Mace Windu, [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin/Legends "Saesee Tiin/Legends") and Plo Koon then set up a rescue mission for the team, with Koon, Tiin, Adi Gallia and Kit Fisto successfully extracting them; however, Piell lost his life.

With the coordinates in the hands of both Ahsoka Tano and Piell's Captain [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin/Legends "Wilhuff Tarkin/Legends"), Yoda decided to meet with Supreme Chancellor Palpatine, as Tano vowed to Piell to give it to the Council, while Tarkin vowed to give it to the Chancellor.

#### Padawan lost[]

Ahsoka Tano vanished in a battle on the world of [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia/Legends "Felucia/Legends"). After some time, a ship piloted by bounty hunters [Sugi](/wiki/Sugi_(bounty_hunter)/Legends "Sugi (bounty hunter)/Legends") and [Seripas](/wiki/Seripas/Legends "Seripas/Legends") came to the Jedi Temple with a band of [Wookiees](/wiki/Wookiee/Legends "Wookiee/Legends"), and two Jedi younglings. Among them was Tano. Yoda and Mace Windu watched as Tano and Anakin Skywalker paid their mutual respects to each other in satisfaction.

#### Mon Calamari[]

:   "*To the Gungans we must look.*"
:   ―Yoda finds reinforcements for their stranded allies.[[48]](#cite_note-Gungan_Attack-48)

Yoda and Mace Windu then made contact with Anakin Skywalker, [Gial Ackbar](/wiki/Gial_Ackbar/Legends "Gial Ackbar/Legends") and Senator Amidala, who were on [Dac](/wiki/Dac/Legends "Dac/Legends") to cool down tensions between the [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari/Legends "Mon Calamari/Legends") and the Separatist-aligned [Quarren](/wiki/Quarren/Legends "Quarren/Legends"). When Kit Fisto and Ahsoka Tano went to aid their forces on the planet, they soon lost contact after the Republic was almost decimated by Separatist commander [Riff Tamson](/wiki/Riff_Tamson/Legends "Riff Tamson/Legends").

As a result of this, the Jedi held a special session to discuss how to proceed. Saesee Tiin suggested that they find a nearby underwater race with an army to aid their allies, and Obi-Wan Kenobi pointed out Naboo. Yoda then contacted the Gungan boss, [Lyonie](/wiki/Lyonie/Legends "Lyonie/Legends"), who dispatched [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks/Legends "Jar Jar Binks/Legends") to lead the army to Mon Cala.

#### Aleen relief mission[]

When several earthquakes struck the [Aleena](/wiki/Aleena/Legends "Aleena/Legends") world of [Aleen](/wiki/Aleen/Legends "Aleen/Legends"), Commander [Wolffe](/wiki/Wolffe/Legends "Wolffe/Legends") and his [team](/wiki/Wolfpack/Legends "Wolfpack/Legends") were sent to the planet with relief supplies as well as Senator Amidala's droids, [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO/Legends "C-3PO/Legends") and [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2/Legends "R2-D2/Legends"). Yoda also appeared in the transmission sent to Wolffe.

#### Rise of the Zygerrian Empire[]

:   "*What is it, Master?*"  
    "*Slavery, a great tool it is for the rise of the Sith.*"
:   ―Plo Koon and Yoda[[49]](#cite_note-Kidnapped-49)

Yoda then made contact with Governor [Roshti](/wiki/Roshti/Legends "Roshti/Legends") of planet [Kiros](/wiki/Kiros/Legends "Kiros/Legends") to warn him that he could not trust Dooku and the Separatist cause. Roshti said it was out of his hands, as the Separatists had already arrived. Yoda promised to send assistance, in the form of Anakin Skywalker, Obi-Wan Kenobi and Ahsoka Tano along with their forces.

Shortly after they won a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Kiros "Battle of Kiros") there, the three appeared in holographic form alongside Admiral [Wullf Yularen](/wiki/Wullf_Yularen/Legends "Wullf Yularen/Legends"), who reported that he ran a scan but found none of the [Togruta](/wiki/Togruta/Legends "Togruta/Legends") colonists—who were not even on the planet.

#### Kenobi's "demise"[]

Criminal mastermind [Moralo Eval](/wiki/Moralo_Eval/Legends "Moralo Eval/Legends") hatched a scheme to abduct Supreme Chancellor Palpatine at the [Festival of Light](/wiki/Festival_of_Light/Legends "Festival of Light/Legends") on Naboo with the aid of Dooku and a cadre of bounty hunters. The Jedi tried to make a deal with Eval for information, to no avail, so devised their own plan to thwart the attack. Obi-Wan Kenobi would fake his death via assassination and pose as the killer to infiltrate Dooku's team and send them information about the attack.

When the deed was done, Yoda attended the [mock funeral](/wiki/Funeral_of_Obi-Wan_Kenobi/Legends "Funeral of Obi-Wan Kenobi/Legends") for Kenobi and later visited with Mace Windu as Kenobi underwent his facial transformation. Yoda and Windu received various communications from Kenobi, and later, he told Anakin Skywalker the truth about Kenobi's "demise." With the aid of Kenobi, Dooku fled, the Chancellor was rescued, and Eval, Cad Bane, [Twazzi](/wiki/Twazzi/Legends "Twazzi/Legends") and [Embo](/wiki/Embo/Legends "Embo/Legends") were apprehended in [Theed](/wiki/Theed/Legends "Theed/Legends").

#### Return of Darth Maul[]
