:   "*Master Yoda, if this is indeed Darth Maul, then his capture is far too important for Obi-Wan to handle alone.*"  
    "*Not alone will Kenobi be; an unexpected ally he may have. Trust the Force we must.*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Yoda discuss Kenobi's ability to defeat Darth Maul[[50]](#cite_note-Revenge-50)

The Jedi later received a transmission that came from the Outer Rim world of [Raydonia](/wiki/Raydonia/Legends "Raydonia/Legends"). To the horror of the Jedi, the person that sent the communication was the presumed dead Sith Lord Darth Maul, the one who murdered Qui-Gon Jinn eleven years before.

Maul said that if Kenobi did not face him, he would destroy the planet, after he [killed](/wiki/Massacre_on_Raydonia/Legends "Massacre on Raydonia/Legends") a group of people in the communication. Kenobi said that he could [defeat](/wiki/Skirmish_above_Raydonia/Legends "Skirmish above Raydonia/Legends") Maul as he once did, and left for Raydonia. Mace Windu expressed his doubts about Kenobi's skill, but Yoda said he may gain an unexpected ally in his quest.

Kenobi returned, and the Jedi learned that Maul had teamed with his brother Savage Opress, the one that massacred the forces at Devaron. Many teams were sent to capture the two [Nightbrothers](/wiki/Nightbrothers/Legends "Nightbrothers/Legends") on many worlds from [Pleem's Nexus](/wiki/Pleem%27s_Nexus "Pleem's Nexus"), [Orto Norwe](/wiki/Orto_Norwe "Orto Norwe"), [Paklan](/wiki/Paklan "Paklan") and [Moorjhone](/wiki/Moorjhone "Moorjhone"). Each Jedi met their end to the two Sith's blades, [Bruu Jun-Fan](/wiki/Bruu_Jun-Fan "Bruu Jun-Fan"), [Ko Solok](/wiki/Ko_Solok "Ko Solok"), [Grohto](/wiki/Grohto "Grohto"), [Judd](/wiki/Judd "Judd") and [Salmara](/wiki/Salmara "Salmara") all lost their lives.

Kenobi and Adi Gallia soon tracked the two Sith from their last known location to [Florrum](/wiki/Florrum/Legends "Florrum/Legends")—where Master Gallia was killed. Yoda, Windu, Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker met with Supreme Chancellor Palpatine to inform him of Maul's return and his plans for the future, but the Chancellor dismissed it, believing that Kenobi took it too personally. Yoda reaffirmed this, but said that when they resurfaced, the Jedi would be swift.

#### Onderon[]

Yoda attended a session of the Jedi Council when [rebels](/wiki/Onderon_rebels/Legends "Onderon rebels/Legends") [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera/Legends "Saw Gerrera/Legends") and [Lux Bonteri](/wiki/Lux_Bonteri/Legends "Lux Bonteri/Legends") sent a transmission with a plea for assistance in the [rebellion](/wiki/Battle_of_Onderon/Legends "Battle of Onderon/Legends") against the Separatist droid army led by the corrupt ruler King [Sanjay Rash](/wiki/Sanjay_Rash/Legends "Sanjay Rash/Legends"), who ousted the [previous monarch](/wiki/Ramsis_Dendup/Legends "Ramsis Dendup/Legends").

The Council said that they would not intervene in their affairs as the planet made their intentions at the start of the war, but promised to send some of their own to train and advise them. Anakin Skywalker, Obi-Wan Kenobi, Ahsoka Tano and Captain [Rex](/wiki/Rex/Legends "Rex/Legends") were sent.

#### The Gathering on Ilum[]

 [![Yoda, the initiates and Padawan Tano on Ilum](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/The_Gathering.png/revision/latest?cb=20121022224325) [![Yoda, the initiates and Padawan Tano on Ilum](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/The_Gathering.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20121022224325)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/The_Gathering.png/revision/latest?cb=20121022224325) 

Yoda, the initiates and Padawan Tano on Ilum

 

Yoda then traveled to Ilum, where he awaited Ahsoka Tano and a clan of initiates who were [deemed ready](/wiki/Gathering_(20_BBY)/Legends "Gathering (20 BBY)/Legends") to construct their own lightsabers in the ancient ritual known as the Gathering. When Tano arrived with the younglings in the [temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_(Ilum)/Legends "Jedi Temple (Ilum)/Legends") there, Yoda showed his own lightsaber and explained to them what they needed to do.

When the younglings went inside to find their own crystal, [Petro](/wiki/Petro/Legends "Petro/Legends") was the first to come out, but Yoda was quick to point out his flaw for certainty and said that he found a crystal, but brought water to them—that is, a *water* crystal. He directed Petro back inside. The other younglings, [Gungi](/wiki/Gungi/Legends "Gungi/Legends"), [Byph](/wiki/Byph/Legends "Byph/Legends"), [Ganodi](/wiki/Ganodi/Legends "Ganodi/Legends"), [Katooni](/wiki/Katooni/Legends "Katooni/Legends") and [Zatt](/wiki/Zatt/Legends "Zatt/Legends"), each came out later. The students then went on to make their personal lightsabers.

#### Attack on the Jedi Temple[]

 [![Yoda presided over the trial of Ahsoka Tano.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Epguide520.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029023559) [![Yoda presided over the trial of Ahsoka Tano.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Epguide520.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131029023559)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Epguide520.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029023559) 

Yoda presided over the trial of Ahsoka Tano.

 

During the peak of the war, [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee/Legends "Barriss Offee/Legends") with the help of [Letta Turmond](/wiki/Letta_Turmond/Legends "Letta Turmond/Legends") [bombed the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar/Legends "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar/Legends") on Coruscant. Yoda then ordered Anakin Skywalker and his Padawan Ahsoka Tano to return from [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia/Legends "Cato Neimoidia/Legends") to help investigate, refusing to trust anyone who was in the temple during the bombing. Yoda's judgement was clouded, but he still guided the Jedi as the leader of the Council.[[51]](#cite_note-TCW:Sabotage-51)

Turmond was captured by Skywalker and Tano. In prison, she requested Tano speak with her, saying Tano was the only one she could trust. When Turmond was strangled to death via the Force, and several clones were murdered by a lightsaber, Republic Admiral [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin/Legends "Wilhuff Tarkin/Legends") accused Tano of being the mastermind responsible for the attack. When Tano escaped the prison, desperate to prove her innocence, Tarkin ordered her captured. This resulted in a manhunt led by Anakin Skywalker and Captain Rex, during which Tano lost her [shoto](/wiki/Shoto_lightsaber/Legends "Shoto lightsaber/Legends")-style lightsaber and escaped.[[52]](#cite_note-TCW:TJWKTM-52)

After Tano eluded her master and fled to the Underworld, Yoda ordered Skywalker and Plo Koon to track her down and bring her to the temple. Tano was quickly captured by Asajj Ventress, now a bounty hunter after having been betrayed by Dooku, who agreed to help the young Padawan in exchange for a pardon for Ventress' crimes as a Sith. Tano contacted Barriss Offee at the Jedi temple. Offee led Tano into a trap by telling her she could find evidence to prove her innocence by going to a warehouse on Level 1315. There, Offee jumped Ventress, stealing her lightsabers and mask. She attacked Tano, knocking her out in front of crates of [nano-droids](/wiki/Nano-droid/Legends "Nano-droid/Legends") and effectively framing her for the bombing.[[53]](#cite_note-TCW:TCAJ-53)

Tano was eventually brought back to the temple, where Yoda reluctantly agreed to expel her from the Jedi Order and have her face a Republic military tribunal before the Senate. Yoda, Obi-Wan Kenobi, Plo Koon, and several other members of the Jedi Council were in the Senate Chambers when Skywalker brought Barriss Offee before the Chancellor, where she confessed to being responsible for the bombings and for framing Tano. In light of this revelation, Yoda and the rest of the Council personally invited Tano to rejoin the Order, but she refused and left. Yoda would regret the Council's decision and began to question the doctrine of the war.[[54]](#cite_note-TCW:The_Wrong_Jedi-54)

#### Clone crisis[]

 [![Yoda speaks with the Council about Tup](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/Yoda_Speaking_To_The_Council.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160302065705) [![Yoda speaks with the Council about Tup](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/Yoda_Speaking_To_The_Council.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160302065705)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/94/Yoda_Speaking_To_The_Council.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160302065705) 

Yoda speaks with the Council about Tup

 

Prior to the war, Darth Sidious and his apprentice, Darth Tyranus, secretly created the Clone Army with the assistance of an unsuspecting [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas/Legends "Sifo-Dyas/Legends"), who had seen visions of a conflict beforehand. When this was done, they had organic [inhibitor chips](/wiki/Inhibitor_chip/Legends "Inhibitor chip/Legends") implanted in their brains. which caused the clones to do anything Palpatine told them to, in this case execute the Jedi. With one simple command, the clones would enter a trance-like state and perform whatever orders they were given.[[55]](#cite_note-TCW:Conspiracy-55)

During the [Battle of Ringo Vinda](/wiki/Battle_of_Ringo_Vinda/Legends "Battle of Ringo Vinda/Legends"), Clone Trooper [Tup](/wiki/Tup/Legends "Tup/Legends") murdered Jedi Master [Tiplar](/wiki/Tiplar/Legends "Tiplar/Legends") when his inhibitor chip was activated prematurely. Sidious ordered Tyranus to apprehend Tup to prevent the Jedi from discovering the truth. Tup was eventually sent to Kamino after Anakin Skywalker, Captain Rex, and [ARC trooper](/wiki/Advanced_Recon_Commando/Legends "Advanced Recon Commando/Legends") [Fives](/wiki/Fives/Legends "Fives/Legends") were able to recover Tup from a Separatist Transport.[[56]](#cite_note-TCW:The_Unknown-56)

After escorting Tup to Kamino, Fives and Rex were greeted by Jedi Master [Shaak Ti](/wiki/Shaak_Ti/Legends "Shaak Ti/Legends"), alongside the main developer of the clones, Kaminoan scientist [Nala Se](/wiki/Nala_Se/Legends "Nala Se/Legends"). Rex returned to Ringo Vinda while Fives remained on Kamino to undergo examination in case Fives had a similar situation. Disputes over the tests led to a debate. While Shaak Ti advised a brain scan, Nala Se suggested terminating the clone and performing an autopsy to isolate the case. Shaak Ti contacted the Jedi Temple where Yoda, alongside Obi-Wan Kenobi, decided Tup should be brought to the temple to be examined through the Force.[[55]](#cite_note-TCW:Conspiracy-55)

What the Jedi were unaware of was that the Kaminoans knew of the inhibitor chips and were working with Count Dooku, who used his Sith name, Tyranus, to prevent the Jedi from making the connection. Dooku ordered that Tup be terminated and that the chip be sent to him to be looked at.[[55]](#cite_note-TCW:Conspiracy-55)

Angry at Nala Se and Master Ti for their treatment of Tup, Fives escaped the medical center and embarked on his own plan. Fives faked leaving the planet, but stayed to try and save Tup and discover the truth. He and the [medical droid](/wiki/Medical_droid/Legends "Medical droid/Legends") [AZI-3](/wiki/AZI-345211896246498721347/Legends "AZI-345211896246498721347/Legends") were able to perform a brain scan on Tup, where they learned of the inhibitor chips. Fives had the droid take the chip out of his and Tup's brains. Unfortunately, the already-weakened Tup died soon after the operation, whispering his last words to Fives.[[55]](#cite_note-TCW:Conspiracy-55) Fives blamed Nala Se for what happened to Tup. Suspecting the Kaminoans of treachery, and with the support of Master Ti, Fives insisted on presenting his evidence and the removed chips directly to Palpatine. Fives was eventually brought to Coruscant, at the request of Shaak Ti, where he was brought before the Chancellor. As the ship landed, Nala Se drugged Fives, causing him to act strange.[[57]](#cite_note-TCW:Fugitive-57)

When Fives attempted to assassinate Palpatine, Yoda and the rest of the Jedi Council ordered Anakin Skywalker to investigate. Fives was killed in the end, and Yoda was ultimately told that the doctors had found another cause, and that a vaccination had been prepared, in case of a future incident.[[58]](#cite_note-TCW:Orders-58)

#### Uncovering the truth[]

:   "*Know now we do that guide the creation of the clones from the beginning, Dooku did. Hm, our enemy created an army for us."  
    "If this was known, public confidence in the war effort, the Jedi, and the Republic would vanish. There would be mass chaos."  
    "Cover up this discovery we must. No one, not even the Chancellor, may know. Valiant men the clones have proven to be. Saved my life and yours they have many times. Believe in them we must. Win the war swiftly we must, before our enemy's designs reach completion, whatever they may be.*"
:   ―Yoda and Mace Windu[[59]](#cite_note-TCW:TLO-59)

Sometime later, the Jedi received a distress signal from a [moon](/wiki/Oba_Diah_moon/Legends "Oba Diah moon/Legends") near [Oba Diah](/wiki/Oba_Diah/Legends "Oba Diah/Legends"). Plo Koon and Commander Wolffe, sent to investigate, found the remains of a shuttle and the lightsaber of Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas, who was killed sometime around the Battle of Naboo while dealing with a conflict on Felucia. Upon reviewing the temple archives, [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu/Legends "Jocasta Nu/Legends") and the Jedi found that the information had been sealed by order of the Supreme Chancellor. While sending Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi to Felucia, Yoda went to speak with Chancellor Palpatine. The latter directed Yoda to Finis Valorum, who had been Supreme Chancellor when these events took place. Anakin and Obi-Wan attempted to communicate with the native tribe on Felucia, but were unable to understand them. They did learn, however, that a second Jedi had shown up with Sifo-Dyas.[[59]](#cite_note-TCW:TLO-59)

 [![Yoda meets with former Supreme Chancellor Finis Valorum on Coruscant.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Valorum_Yoda_The_Lost_One.png/revision/latest?cb=20140914220905) [![Yoda meets with former Supreme Chancellor Finis Valorum on Coruscant.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Valorum_Yoda_The_Lost_One.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140914220905)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Valorum_Yoda_The_Lost_One.png/revision/latest?cb=20140914220905) 

Yoda meets with former Supreme Chancellor Finis Valorum on Coruscant.

 

Valorum told Yoda that he sent Sifo-Dyas to negotiate with the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate/Legends "Pyke Syndicate/Legends") to stop a booming drug trade underneath Coruscant. Valorum also revealed that he kept this secret, fearing his opponents in the bureaucracy. The talks were postponed after the Council sent Sifo-Dyas to intervene on Felucia. Valorum was unable to identify the second Jedi, but did say that his assistant, [Silman](/wiki/Silman/Legends "Silman/Legends"), was with Sifo-Dyas when he was shot down.[[59]](#cite_note-TCW:TLO-59)

Eventually, Yoda dispatched Anakin and Obi-Wan to Oba Diah, where they learned the Pykes were paid to shoot down the ship carrying Sifo-Dyas, but had kept Silman captive as leverage and that Dooku was in fact the individual known as Tyranus, leading them to realize Dooku impersonated Sifo-Dyas to help push forward the Clone Wars. Yoda, not knowing how to stop the plot, suggested the Jedi keep the discovery a secret, and that they should keep playing the Sith Lord's game.[[59]](#cite_note-TCW:TLO-59)

#### Discovering immortality[]

 [![Yoda hears the voice of Qui-Gon Jinn.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/YodaHearsQui-Gon.png/revision/latest?cb=20140713170416) [![Yoda hears the voice of Qui-Gon Jinn.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/YodaHearsQui-Gon.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140713170416)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/YodaHearsQui-Gon.png/revision/latest?cb=20140713170416) 

Yoda hears the voice of Qui-Gon Jinn.

 

While meditating during the end of the war, Yoda heard the voice of Qui-Gon Jinn, who demonstrated his presence by levitating Yoda. The encounter left Yoda distracted during the subsequent Council gathering, leaving them worried about whether the stresses of the war were finally taking its toll on him. While strolling through the Temple gardens, Yoda was greeted by Anakin. Yoda asked him about his encounter with Qui-Gon's spirit on [Mortis](/wiki/Mortis/Legends "Mortis/Legends"), which Anakin had dismissed as a trick, noting the Jedi belief that one could not retain their identity after becoming one with the Force. Yoda responded that he now questioned this dogma.[[60]](#cite_note-TCW:Voices-60)

Yoda confessed what happened to the Council, much to their disbelief. They agreed though to meditate with him, to verify his experience. Despite meditating together for an entire day, they were unable to hear anything. [Ki-Adi Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi/Legends "Ki-Adi-Mundi/Legends") expressed worry that Yoda had become susceptible to Sith manipulation, so Yoda underwent medical tests that revealed that he was still in good health. Jedi Doctor [Rig Nema](/wiki/Rig_Nema/Legends "Rig Nema/Legends") suggested Yoda undergo a [deprivation ritual](/wiki/Deprivation_ritual/Legends "Deprivation ritual/Legends") that would allow him to meditate more strongly and find the source of the voice.[[60]](#cite_note-TCW:Voices-60)

Agreeing, Yoda was suspended in a liquid tank with an [oxygen mask](/wiki/Breath_mask/Legends "Breath mask/Legends") to bring him as close as possible to death without actually becoming one with the Force. While unconscious, Qui-Gon's voice requested Yoda go to [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah/Legends "Dagobah/Legends"), and to tell no one about it. After, Obi-Wan broke open the tank due to his concern over Yoda's failing life signs.[[60]](#cite_note-TCW:Voices-60)

Put on bedrest and under guard, Yoda convinced Anakin to help him escape by posing as simply accompanying each other for a walk. Guided to the Jedi Temple Hangar, Anakin lent Yoda his [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid/Legends "Astromech droid/Legends") R2-D2 to accompany him to his [personal interceptor](/wiki/Eta-2_Actis-class_interceptor/Legends "Eta-2 Actis-class interceptor/Legends"). Yoda and R2-D2 flew to Dagobah, where Yoda asked the droid to stay with their ship while he found a clearing to meditate.[[60]](#cite_note-TCW:Voices-60)

 [![Yoda communes with Qui-Gon on Dagobah.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bc/YodaDagobahLight.png/revision/latest?cb=20140825120811) [![Yoda communes with Qui-Gon on Dagobah.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bc/YodaDagobahLight.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140825120811)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bc/YodaDagobahLight.png/revision/latest?cb=20140825120811) 

Yoda communes with Qui-Gon on Dagobah.

 

Qui-Gon's voice greeted him. Yoda asked why he could not see him. Qui-Gon explained he had not been fully trained enough to do so. The Living Force appeared to Yoda in the form of [fireflies](/wiki/Firefly/Legends "Firefly/Legends"), guiding Yoda to a [cave](/wiki/Cave_of_Evil/Legends "Cave of Evil/Legends") strong with the dark side, it showed the Jedi Master a vision of the future, where a hooded Sith Lord slaughtered the Jedi. Qui-Gon explained to a distraught Yoda that he would help him bring hope for the future, and directed him to the planet that spawned the midi-chlorians.[[60]](#cite_note-TCW:Voices-60)[[61]](#cite_note-TCW:Destiny-61)

Arriving there, Yoda gave his lightsaber to R2-D2 for safekeeping, and descended into the world to meet the [Force Priestesses](/wiki/Force_Priestesses/Legends "Force Priestesses/Legends"), who agreed to teach him how to achieve life after death. First, Yoda confronted a manifestation of his own dark side, conquering his hubris. Next, he witnessed a vision of the Jedi massacred in the Temple, where an apparition of Katooni invited him to enter a peaceful courtyard to escape these painful events. Seeing Qui-Gon, Kenobi, Ahsoka and Dooku together, alive and full Jedi, Yoda recognized the vision's falsehood, overcoming its temptation and his attachment to those that have fallen.[[61]](#cite_note-TCW:Destiny-61)

 [![Yoda sees the specter of Darth Bane.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/EpGuide613.png/revision/latest?cb=20190421115621) [![Yoda sees the specter of Darth Bane.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/EpGuide613.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190421115621)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c7/EpGuide613.png/revision/latest?cb=20190421115621) 

Yoda sees the specter of Darth Bane.

 

Instructed to complete his tests on the Sith homeworld of [Moraband](/wiki/Korriban/Legends "Korriban/Legends"), Yoda and R2-D2 [flew](/wiki/Mission_to_Moraband/Legends "Mission to Moraband/Legends") to the [valley](/wiki/Valley_of_the_Dark_Lords/Legends "Valley of the Dark Lords/Legends") where the ancient Sith Lords were buried. Recognizing the danger, Yoda instructed R2-D2 to return to the Jedi Temple and inform the Council of what happened, if he did not come back after three nights. Spectres of a serpent, [undead](/wiki/Zombie/Legends "Zombie/Legends") Sith warriors and even [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane/Legends "Darth Bane/Legends") himself confronted him, but Yoda brushed them off. As he entered a temple execution chamber, the Force Priestesses warned Yoda that whatever he encountered there would be beyond their control.[[62]](#cite_note-TCW:Sacrifice-62)

Unknown to Yoda, Darth Sidious and Dooku sensed his presence on Moraband, and met in an abandoned tower in the industrial sector of Coruscant. Using Dooku and Yoda's [Force bond](/wiki/Force-bond/Legends "Force-bond/Legends"), Sidious planned to reach out to Yoda and crush his spirit. Appearing to Yoda in the form of Sifo-Dyas, Sidious had Yoda wake up in a [Republic attack gunship](/wiki/Low_Altitude_Assault_Transport/infantry/Legends "Low Altitude Assault Transport/infantry/Legends") with Anakin and members of the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion/Legends "501st Legion/Legends"), en route to terminate the Sith on Coruscant. As they arrived, the clones, led by Captain Rex, rushed at Dooku only to be hit with Sith lightning. Anakin immediately attacked Dooku while Sidious fled. Walking sadly past the fallen clones, a dismayed Yoda witnessed Anakin decapitate Dooku. However, he left Anakin and pursued Sidious.[[62]](#cite_note-TCW:Sacrifice-62)

Emerging on a catwalk, Yoda and Sidious ignited their lightsabers and engaged in a fierce duel that took them further away from the industrial tower. Anakin eventually caught up with the pair, engaging Sidious in lightsaber combat alongside the Grand Master. Yoda was able to throw Sidious away from them with a Force push, but Anakin foolishly took the chance to attack Sidious while he was still on the ground. The Dark Lord rose to his feet and immediately proceeded to Force-choke Anakin before rendering him unconscious with Force lightning. Sidious then turned his lightning upon Yoda, who immediately began to deflect it with his bare hands by using tutaminis, advancing upon Sidious and closing the gap between them. Although both struggled with the effort of overcoming the other, Yoda was able to cause Sidious to begin to slowly reel backwards with the strength of his counterattack before the combination of their powers caused an explosion that blasted them apart. Sidious was sent toppling over the catwalk's banisters while Yoda was able to maintain his ground. Yoda immediately looked for a seemingly vanished Sidious only to witness the latter damaging the catwalk with his lightsaber from below. Yoda leapt after him, but Yoda's attention soon became divided between Force-lifting Anakin to save him from falling to his death and blocking Sidious' Sith lightning with his lightsaber. After Sidious taunted him by suggesting he sacrifice Anakin to concentrate on defeating him, Yoda put down his lightsaber to ensure Anakin's safety only to be hit with lightning. As the catwalk collapsed, Yoda maneuvered Anakin to safety and prevented Sidious escaping by severing the collapsing catwalk with his lightsaber, dragging Sidious down too. The incident proved Yoda's selflessness and demonstrated his resolve to Sidious, who concluded the illusion as he realized it would take more to defeat the Jedi Master.[[62]](#cite_note-TCW:Sacrifice-62)

Yoda awoke and was greeted by a Priestess, who explained he would continue his training with Qui-Gon's spirit. As she disappeared in a glow of light, Yoda had a vision of the future, including his own death.[[63]](#cite_note-SW-Sacrifice_Episode_Gallery-63) Yoda returned to the Jedi Temple, where Windu and Kenobi greeted him in the garden. Yoda claimed his journey had been uneventful, but wondered if Jedi had been wrong to wage the war on the Republic's behalf.[[62]](#cite_note-TCW:Sacrifice-62) (Though, despite his fears, he never gave up opposing the Sith.)[[64]](#cite_note-ROTJn-64)[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_novelization-65)

#### Vjun[]

 [![Yoda during the ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/MissionToVjun.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070605202243) [![Yoda during the ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/MissionToVjun.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20070605202243)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/26/MissionToVjun.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070605202243) 

Yoda during the [mission to Vjun](/wiki/Mission_to_Vjun_(Clone_Wars) "Mission to Vjun (Clone Wars)")

 

Near the end of the war, Yoda journeyed to the planet [Vjun](/wiki/Vjun/Legends "Vjun/Legends") after receiving a communication from Count Dooku, stating his intention to defect. Although Yoda was well aware of Dooku's treachery, he could not help but hope the count's plea was sincere, and that his former student was, at last, trying to find his way home.

Taking Jedi Masters [Maks Leem](/wiki/Maks_Leem "Maks Leem"), [Jai Maruk](/wiki/Jai_Maruk "Jai Maruk"), and their Padawans [Whie Malreaux](/wiki/Whie_Malreaux/Legends "Whie Malreaux/Legends") and [Tallisibeth Enwandung-Esterhazy](/wiki/Tallisibeth_Enwandung-Esterhazy "Tallisibeth Enwandung-Esterhazy"), Yoda traveled secretly to Vjun. However, along the way, Asajj Ventress tracked and captured the foursome, and unleashed new assassin droids. Killing Leem and Maruk, Ventress tried to destroy the [space station](/wiki/Phindar_Spaceport "Phindar Spaceport") to kill Yoda. The little green creature, using the help of his [media doppelgänger](/wiki/Palleus_Chuff "Palleus Chuff"), destroyed Ventress' [ship](/wiki/Last_Call_(Ginivex-class) "Last Call (Ginivex-class)"), allowing them to escape. Yoda rendezvoused with Dooku in [Château Malreaux](/wiki/Ch%C3%A2teau_Malreaux "Château Malreaux") and confronted the Sith Lord over his choice to join the dark side. Dooku attempted to convert Yoda, but the Jedi Master easily pushed aside Dooku's hollow promises. Instead, Yoda tried to persuade Dooku to rejoin the Jedi Order, and it appeared his words had a profound effect on Dooku. The unexpected intervention of Obi-Wan Kenobi and Anakin Skywalker hardened Dooku's resolve, however, and Yoda was forced into a second duel with the count. Just as their duel on Geonosis, Yoda's fallen apprentice showed proficiency in lightsaber combat nigh akin to his own, even managed to pierce the Jedi Grandmaster's centuries worth of lightsaber knowledge by delivering a small blow that passed by his defenses. Both Yoda and Dooku survived, but each left the confrontation once again before the victor could be determined with much on their minds.[[11]](#cite_note-Yoda:_Dark_Rendezvous-11)

#### Argul[]

When fierce [fighting](/wiki/Battle_of_Argul "Battle of Argul") broke out on the planet [Argul](/wiki/Argul "Argul"), Yoda traveled to the world with a number of other Jedi, to help evacuate refugees from Argul's cities. However, there were not enough transports for the Jedi to evacuate all of the [Argullians](/wiki/Argullian "Argullian"), so Yoda left the planet, promising to return with more ships.[[66]](#cite_note-OtF-66)

**This section of the article assumes a specific path in a roleplaying adventure. Alternate paths may be noted in the "[Behind the scenes](#Behind_the_scenes)" section. The events in this section may or may not have been confirmed as [canonical](/wiki/Canon "Canon") within the [*Star Wars* Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") continuity.**

Yoda commandeered the [Sullustan task force](/wiki/Sullustan_task_force "Sullustan task force") and returned to Argul with the fleet, using it to reinforce Republic forces on the planet. The task force quickly turned the tide of the battle in the favor of the Republic, and Yoda landed with the reinforcements, via a gunship. He then congratulated the surviving Jedi on the world, for their efforts during the battle.[[66]](#cite_note-OtF-66)

Assumption ends here.

#### Bpfasshi Dark Jedi crisis[]

Early in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY/Legends "19 BBY/Legends"), Yoda led a Jedi task force to confront the [Dark Jedi](/wiki/Dark_Jedi/Legends "Dark Jedi/Legends") crisis on the planet [Bpfassh](/wiki/Bpfassh "Bpfassh"). A group of [Bpfasshi](/wiki/Bpfasshi/Legends "Bpfasshi/Legends") Dark Jedi were responsible for a rampage of terror and destruction throughout the [Bpfassh system](/wiki/Bpfassh_system/Legends "Bpfassh system/Legends") and, indeed, the entire [Sluis sector](/wiki/Sluis_sector/Legends "Sluis sector/Legends"). The task force was able to stop the insurrection and quell the uprising.[[67]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Rebellion_(video_game)-67) Yoda then personally engaged the last of the Bpfasshi Dark Jedi, who survived the Jedi intervention and managed to escape, commandeering [Jorj Car'das](/wiki/Jorj_Car%27das "Jorj Car'das")'s smuggling ship, in a duel that lasted a day and a half, before finally defeating him[[68]](#cite_note-VotF-68)—or so it seemed. Mortally wounded, the fallen Bpfasshi Jedi made it to the swamp planet [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah/Legends "Dagobah/Legends"), where he died.[[69]](#cite_note-holocron-69) At the site of the Dark Jedi's death, a dark-side nexus was formed, becoming the Dark Side Cave.[[70]](#cite_note-HeirtotheEmpire-70)

### Rise of the Sith Lords[]

#### Battle of Coruscant[]

:   "*Strange is the enemy's strategy.*"  
    "*A massive invasion but no attempt to take the temple or senate.*"  
    "*Unless an elaborate distraction.*"  
    "*To hide their primary objective.*"  
    "*Palpatine!*"
:   ―Yoda and [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu/Legends "Mace Windu/Legends")[[71]](#cite_note-CW25-71)

Despite these dark sojourns, Yoda largely remained on Coruscant and coordinated the war effort on behalf of the Jedi. He did, however, journey to [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia/Legends "Cato Neimoidia/Legends") shortly before the [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant/Legends "Battle of Coruscant/Legends") to investigate the discovery of Nute Gunray's [mechno-chair](/wiki/Mechno-chair/Legends "Mechno-chair/Legends").[[72]](#cite_note-Labyrinth_of_Evil-72)

During the Battle of Coruscant, Yoda again rode his kybuck into battle, to support the forces of [Captain Fordo](/wiki/Fordo "Fordo") with a dazzling display of [mounted lightsaber combat](/wiki/Mounted_lightsaber_combat "Mounted lightsaber combat"). He eventually sent the creature back to the Temple, and continued to fight, side by side with Mace Windu, on foot.[[26]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Clone_Wars-26)

 [![Yoda and Mace Windu realize  during the attack on Coruscant.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/YodaMaceCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100323180403) [![Yoda and Mace Windu realize  during the attack on Coruscant.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/YodaMaceCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20100323180403)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/YodaMaceCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100323180403) 

Yoda and Mace Windu realize [who the Separatists are after](/wiki/Palpatine/Legends "Palpatine/Legends") during the attack on Coruscant.

 

Despite their efforts, the Jedi were unable to prevent the capture of Supreme Chancellor Palpatine by [General](/wiki/General/Legends "General/Legends") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous/Legends "Grievous/Legends"), though Anakin Skywalker and Obi-Wan Kenobi later rescued him and killed Dooku in the process. With his hopes of converting his pupil back to the light dashed, Yoda set his focus on tracking down the last Sith Lord, though tensions between the Jedi High Council and the [Office of the Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Office_of_the_Supreme_Chancellor/Legends "Office of the Supreme Chancellor/Legends") were high.[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_novelization-65)

In 19 BBY, Supreme Chancellor Palpatine appointed Anakin to the Jedi Council as his own representative. Again, the Council was hesitant about Skywalker's temperament but, in turn, acquiesced to the request. Yoda once more played a significant role in the young Jedi's ascension in the order, as they denied Anakin the rank of Jedi Master. During that discussion, the clones reported that the Wookiees were under attack, and Yoda, having once been the planet's [watchman](/wiki/Jedi_Watchman/Legends "Jedi Watchman/Legends"), decided to venture to Kashyyyk to assist them.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

#### Invasion of Kashyyyk[]

:   "*I fear the dark cloud of the Sith shrouds us all.*"
:   ―Yoda[[27]](#cite_note-CW20-27)

 [![Yoda observing the ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Overlooking_the_Chaos.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210050128) [![Yoda observing the ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Overlooking_the_Chaos.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130210050128)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/Overlooking_the_Chaos.png/revision/latest?cb=20130210050128) 

Yoda observing the [Battle of Kashyyyk](/wiki/Battle_of_Kashyyyk/Legends "Battle of Kashyyyk/Legends")

 

Yoda was quite skilled in the technique of [battle meditation](/wiki/Battle_meditation/Legends "Battle meditation/Legends") and would use this to some effect during the [Battle of Kashyyyk](/wiki/Battle_of_Kashyyyk/Legends "Battle of Kashyyyk/Legends"), assisting the Wookiees and clones as they fought the Separatist army.[[73]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-73)

While Yoda was on Kashyyyk, Darth Sidious ordered the clones to execute [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66/Legends "Order 66/Legends"), which meant the extermination of all Jedi. Yoda sensed his Jedi brethren being killed all over the galaxy and, coming to the only logical conclusion for so many concurrent deaths of his fellow Jedi, he suddenly realized, in one horrible instant, that the clone troopers were responsible. Worst of all, before the attack began, he felt Anakin Skywalker's ascension into Sidious's new apprentice, Darth Vader. Despite being filled with grief, he was still able to defend himself, [decapitating](/wiki/Sai_cha/Legends "Sai cha/Legends") [Commander](/wiki/Clone_Commander/Legends "Clone Commander/Legends") [Gree](/wiki/Gree_(clone_trooper)/Legends "Gree (clone trooper)/Legends") and [his assistant](/wiki/Unidentified_clone_scout_trooper "Unidentified clone scout trooper") with a single strike and stop the rest of [his former troops](/wiki/9th_Assault_Corps/Legends "9th Assault Corps/Legends") from assassinating him. With help from the Wookiees [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca/Legends "Chewbacca/Legends") and [Tarfful](/wiki/Tarfful/Legends "Tarfful/Legends"), Yoda, like fellow Jedi [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos/Legends "Quinlan Vos/Legends"), survived and was able to escape to meet with another surviving Jedi Master, Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Senator Bail Organa of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan/Legends "Alderaan/Legends").

#### Dark revelations[]

:   "*In a dark place we find ourselves… and a little more knowledge might light our way.*"
:   ―Yoda[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

Yoda and Kenobi then [went](/wiki/Infiltration_of_the_Jedi_Temple/Legends "Infiltration of the Jedi Temple/Legends") to the conquered Jedi Temple so they could reconfigure the emanating signal that was drawing Jedi survivors back to Coruscant into a trap. They disabled the deadly beacon after cutting through several clone troopers, and saw the Temple littered with the bodies of fallen Jedi, including younglings, who had been slaughtered with a lightsaber.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

 [![Yoda fights his way into the , now in the hands of the .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Pg3_saber_bg.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20051109050907) [![Yoda fights his way into the , now in the hands of the .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Pg3_saber_bg.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20051109050907)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Pg3_saber_bg.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20051109050907) 

Yoda fights his way into the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple/Legends "Jedi Temple/Legends"), now in the hands of the [Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire/Legends "Galactic Empire/Legends").

 

As Kenobi finished recalibrating the coded signal, he felt he must know who was responsible for the attack. Yoda, knowing that the revelation of Anakin's turn to the dark side would cause Kenobi pain, cautioned him before his fellow Master activated the security recordings. As they watched, they learned of Palpatine's Sith identity and that the Republic was now a [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire/Legends "Galactic Empire/Legends"). They agreed that the two Sith Lords needed to be destroyed. Yoda would remain on Coruscant to confront the newly crowned Emperor in the [Senate Building](/wiki/Senate_Building/Legends "Senate Building/Legends"), while a deeply reluctant Kenobi would battle his former apprentice.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

#### Duel in the Senate[]

:   "*I have waited a long time for this moment, my little green friend… at last, the Jedi are no more.*"  
    "*Not if anything to say about it, I have! […] At an end your rule is, and not short enough it was.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious and Yoda[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

As Sidious waited for word from his apprentice, Yoda entered the office. Quickly dispatching Sidious' guards by Force-pushing them into the wall, Yoda confronted the Sith Lord, who seemed surprised at his survival and attacked Yoda with Force lightning. Yoda quickly fought back with a [Force push](/wiki/Telekinesis/Legends "Telekinesis/Legends") that sent the Sith Lord across the room and into his chair, where he fell onto the ground in a crumpled heap. As Sidious tried to flee, Yoda jumped in front of him and pulled out his lightsaber. Sidious then drew his own lightsaber, and the duel began.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

 [![Yoda and Darth Sidious  in the .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b4/YodaDuel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091201195359) [![Yoda and Darth Sidious  in the .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b4/YodaDuel.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20091201195359)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b4/YodaDuel.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091201195359) 

Yoda and Darth Sidious [duel](/wiki/Skirmish_in_the_Senate "Skirmish in the Senate") in the [Grand Convocation Chamber](/wiki/Grand_Convocation_Chamber "Grand Convocation Chamber").

 

The [duel moved into the Senate](/wiki/Skirmish_in_the_Senate "Skirmish in the Senate"), where the two Force users engaged in a saber duel in the Chancellor's podium. The two at first stalemated each other, but Yoda ultimately started to gain the upper hand, pressuring Sidious by using his small size to easily avoid the latter's strikes and to nimbly navigate through the podium,[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6) whereas Sidious was hampered by the podium's tight space. Not allowing a moment's rest for Sidious, Yoda flurried around the Sith with his centuries worth of lightsaber knowledge, hitting with pristine determination to end this here and now. Eventually, Yoda [dislodged](/wiki/Sun_djem/Legends "Sun djem/Legends") the Dark Lord's lightsaber from his grip and would have slain the Sith if not for a desperate bolt of Sith lightning forcing him back.[[74]](#cite_note-ROTS_junior_novel-74) After retreating to the surrounding Senate pods, Sidious changed tactics and began using the Force to hurl several Senate Hoverpods at him from above, forcing Yoda to concentrate on dodging the improvised projectiles instead of getting to Sidious's level. The [Grand Master of the Jedi Order](/wiki/Grand_Master/Legends "Grand Master/Legends") and the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith/Legends "Dark Lord of the Sith/Legends") were counterpoised.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

As the duel progressed, during a match between the embodiments of the light and the dark, Yoda realized the Jedi had lost the war before it even started. In the last millennium, the Sith had changed and adapted, becoming a new entity; while the Jedi Order, under his leadership, spent the same time merely training to re-fight the *last* war. Moreso, he sensed that while he was weakening, Sidious was only growing stronger. Hence, Yoda realized that the longer the duel continued, the greater the gap between his power and Sidious' would become. For while both of them were elderly avatars of the dark and light side, Yoda was ancient at nearly 900 years while Sidious, still old, stood at the beginning of his 60s. If he was to win at all, he had to end the duel, and quickly.[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_novelization-65) As Sidious continued his telekinetic assault, Yoda caught one of the Senate podiums and flung it back at Sidious, who leapt out of its path to a lower Senate pod. Yoda took the opportunity to engage the distracted Dark Lord at close quarters once again, but Sidious fired a torrent of Force lightning at Yoda. The attack tore Yoda's lightsaber from his hand, and the diminutive Jedi was forced to use tutaminis to withstand the Dark Lord's lightning.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6) As Sidious increased the power of his lightning and aimed his attack above Yoda's defense by elevating his body, Yoda began to falter. As Sidious intensified his attack further, the Jedi Master's vision pierced the veil of the dark side, and he was able to see a glimpse of the future. What he might have seen was unclear, but Yoda's vision certainly did reveal to him that, if the galaxy were ever to be free of the Sith, he had to remain alive.[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_novelization-65)

Yoda's newfound hope gave him the strength to resist Sidious's might, and he quickly managed to [coalesce](/wiki/Force_deflection "Force deflection") the energy of Sidious' lightning into a blue orb, slowly redirecting it back to an astounded Sidious, who was slowly being pushed back by the strength of Yoda's counterattack. But just as Yoda appeared to be on the brink of succeeding, the combination of both of their powers caused the orb to explode, and the blast blew them both apart, ending the battle. Both Masters were able to grasp the edge of nearby Senate pods, with Sidious barely managing to right himself and achieve the high ground. Yoda, however, was unable to maintain his grasp, and fell to the floor of the Senate Chamber. Realizing that any chance he had to defeat Sidious was gone with his stamina exhausted and his body battered, Yoda decided to flee and escaped through several service pipes, with his small size proving advantageous in this moment, and met up with Bail Organa, who hurried him away in [his speeder](/wiki/XJ-2_airspeeder "XJ-2 airspeeder") as Yoda mused about his failure. The two left for the [asteroid](/wiki/Asteroid/Legends "Asteroid/Legends") colony of [Polis Massa](/wiki/Polis_Massa/Legends "Polis Massa/Legends").[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

### Exile ([19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY/Legends "19 BBY/Legends")–[4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY/Legends "4 ABY/Legends"))[]

:   "*Into exile I must go. Failed, I have.*"
:   ―Yoda to [Bail Prestor Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa/Legends "Bail Prestor Organa/Legends")[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

 [![Yoda surveys , his new home.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/YodaLandsonDagobah.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130808194347) [![Yoda surveys , his new home.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/YodaLandsonDagobah.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20130808194347)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0c/YodaLandsonDagobah.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130808194347) 

Yoda surveys [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah/Legends "Dagobah/Legends"), his new home.

 

On Polis Massa, Yoda communed with the spirit of Qui-Gon Jinn, who agreed to train Yoda in secret [Whill](/wiki/Ancient_Order_of_the_Whills "Ancient Order of the Whills") techniques he had learned after his death. He also regrouped with Kenobi, who had defeated but not killed Vader. Kenobi brought with him a badly injured Amidala, who was treated in Polis Massa. Although Amidala bore twins, Luke and [Leia](/wiki/Leia_Organa_Solo/Legends "Leia Organa Solo/Legends"), she died soon afterward. Yoda decided that the babies were strong in the Force.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)
When returning to the [*Sundered Heart*](/wiki/Sundered_Heart/Legends "Sundered Heart/Legends") with Bail Organa and reuniting with Obi-Wan Kenobi, he decided that Luke and Leia—the Skywalker children—should be hidden from Darth Vader and Darth Sidious in secret locations. Other than the ancient Jedi Master, only the Organas, the Lars, and Kenobi would know of their placement. He also told Obi-Wan that an old friend, Master Qui-Gon Jinn, had found a way to retain one's consciousness after death, and would teach both of them this skill. Yoda would take on a role he had not played in centuries: that of an apprentice.[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_novelization-65)

During the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge/Legends "Great Jedi Purge/Legends"), Yoda stowed away aboard an automated Polis Massan–registered barge that was transporting grain to starving inhabitants of the ex-Separatist world of [Sluis Van](/wiki/Sluis_Van/Legends "Sluis Van/Legends"). The ship briefly dropped out of hyperspace near the planet Dagobah. Undetected and unrecorded, Yoda launched [his escape pod](/wiki/E3-standard_starship_lifeboat/Legends "E3-standard starship lifeboat/Legends") and landed on the swamp planet. He would spend his entire exile hiding on Dagobah, from the onset of the [Dark Times](/wiki/Imperial_Era/Legends "Imperial Era/Legends") to the early period of the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War/Legends "Galactic Civil War/Legends").[[75]](#cite_note-e3lifeboatdatabank-75)

 [![Yoda experiences a vision of Darth Sidious in the Dark Side Cave](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/TheCave-SWGs7.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120219041130) [![Yoda experiences a vision of Darth Sidious in the Dark Side Cave](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/TheCave-SWGs7.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20120219041130)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/82/TheCave-SWGs7.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120219041130) 

Yoda experiences a vision of Darth Sidious in the Dark Side Cave

 

Yoda soon found and healed the badly wounded smuggler Jorj Car'das, who had been wounded by a survivor of the Bpfasshi Dark Jedi insurrection.[[68]](#cite_note-VotF-68) After a revived Car'das left Dagobah, Yoda made [his home](/wiki/Yoda%27s_Hut/Legends "Yoda's Hut/Legends") near the Dark Side Cave, which, in addition to the massive number of lifeforms (which masked his presence in the Living Force), counteracted his presence in the light side. Yoda's imprint on the Force was hidden, as was his sanctuary from the Emperor's sinister agents.[[70]](#cite_note-HeirtotheEmpire-70) Moreover, Dagobah was one of the thirty-seven planets erased from the Jedi Archives, further ensuring his anonymity.

At some point, he encountered [the Children](/wiki/The_Children "The Children"), a group of cannibals whose parents had been part of a Republic survey team that became stranded on the planet decades earlier. For some reason, the Children became extremely afraid of him and called him the "Imp."[[76]](#cite_note-Galaxy_of_Fear:_The_Hunger-76)

Shortly afterward, [Qu Rahn](/wiki/Qu_Rahn/Legends "Qu Rahn/Legends"), another Jedi who survived both Order 66 and its aftermath, went to Dagobah and was taught many skills by the old master. Before the [Battle of Hoth](/wiki/Battle_of_Hoth/Legends "Battle of Hoth/Legends"), [Tash](/wiki/Tash_Arranda/Legends "Tash Arranda/Legends") and [Zak Arranda](/wiki/Zak_Arranda/Legends "Zak Arranda/Legends") also encountered Yoda.[[76]](#cite_note-Galaxy_of_Fear:_The_Hunger-76) It was during these years that the diminutive being developed a taste for [rootleaf stew](/wiki/Rootleaf_stew/Legends "Rootleaf stew/Legends").

When [Starkiller](/wiki/Subject_1138 "Subject 1138"), a clone of Darth Vader's deceased [secret apprentice](/wiki/Galen_Marek "Galen Marek"), traveled to Dagobah to meditate, he discovered the entrance to a cave. Before entering, Starkiller met Yoda, although he was oblivious to the diminutive creature's identity. Despite his vague comments, Yoda assured the clone that his path clearly brought him to the cave and venturing inside would yield some answers for him. After Starkiller exited the cave, Yoda told him that he had to follow his destiny, to which the clone said he would follow it to the ends of the galaxy.

 [![Yoda practices his lightsaber skills in exile on Dagobah.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/db/Yoda_2014_NationalChampionship_PrizeCard.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423035458) [![Yoda practices his lightsaber skills in exile on Dagobah.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/db/Yoda_2014_NationalChampionship_PrizeCard.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20180423035458)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/db/Yoda_2014_NationalChampionship_PrizeCard.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423035458) 

Yoda practices his lightsaber skills in exile on Dagobah.

 

By this time, Emperor Palpatine increased the bounty on Yoda by a further 30,000 [credits](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard/Legends "Galactic Credit Standard/Legends").[[77]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Force_Unleashed_II-77) Due to multiple attempts at collecting the reward through fraud, the Empire had to modify the conditions so that no one else would be tempted to cheat the Empire. First, the reward was only good for a living subject. Second, a non-negotiable death penalty was attached to the bounty and would be enforced on anyone who tried to collect the reward by handing over a "false Yoda." The Empire also used the fate of [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter/Legends "Bounty hunter/Legends") [Rurrk Ca'rivv](/wiki/Rurrk_Ca%27rivv "Rurrk Ca'rivv") to remind others that Imperial authorities were quite capable of telling the difference between a Jedi Master of advanced age and a dead [Jawa](/wiki/Jawa/Legends "Jawa/Legends") stripped of his clothing and surgically altered, noting the smell as the first and most obvious sign of deception. Shortly thereafter, Yoda was listed one of eight of the Empire's most wanted criminals, alongside Alderaanian [Princess](/wiki/Princess/Legends "Princess/Legends") Leia Organa, former Mon Calamari senator [Meena Tills](/wiki/Meena_Tills/Legends "Meena Tills/Legends"), and Obi-Wan Kenobi, of which they were often issued in recruitment videos for stormtroopers and the Imperial Army.[[78]](#cite_note-Be_a_Stormtrooper:_part_1-78)

One day around [0 BBY](/wiki/0_BBY/Legends "0 BBY/Legends"), Jorj Car'das suddenly showed up once more on Dagobah, violently demanding that Yoda put his failing health right. Yoda simply took his blaster and the [beckon call](/wiki/Beckon_call/Legends "Beckon call/Legends") from his ship and flung them into the swamp, then berated Car'das for wasting the second chance he had been given. He also told Car'das that he couldn't help him any further, since he was busy preparing for the most important training he would ever lead. Car'das became so embarrassed by his own actions that he couldn't return to his group, so he fled to [Exocron](/wiki/Exocron "Exocron"), where Yoda had indicated he might receive help from the [Aing-Tii](/wiki/Aing-Tii/Legends "Aing-Tii/Legends") monks.[[68]](#cite_note-VotF-68)
At some point during his exile, Alliance historian Major [Arhul Hextrophon](/wiki/Arhul_Hextrophon/Legends "Arhul Hextrophon/Legends") discovered Yoda's whereabouts and traveled to Dagobah to find him. Yoda originally intended to wipe his mind but in the end decided against it, since it was not the Jedi way to cause pain and suffering—in this case, through the loss of memory. Hextrophon was instead made to swear not to reveal his existence. He erased the records which led him to Yoda in the first place, and apart from keeping logs in his private journal, it is believed he kept his word.[[79]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Sourcebook-79)

#### The next Skywalker[]

:   "*Try not. Do, or do not. There is no try.*"
:   ―Yoda to Luke Skywalker — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/fc/ThereIsNoTry-ESB.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250405134841)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:ThereIsNoTry-ESB.flac "File:ThereIsNoTry-ESB.flac"))[[4]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_V:_The_Empire_Strikes_Back-4)

 [![Yoda passes down his knowledge to Luke Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Yodalukedagobah.png/revision/latest?cb=20130324024419) [![Yoda passes down his knowledge to Luke Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Yodalukedagobah.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130324024419)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Yodalukedagobah.png/revision/latest?cb=20130324024419) 

Yoda passes down his knowledge to Luke Skywalker.

 

When Luke Skywalker, son of Anakin Skywalker, arrived on Dagobah, Yoda met him but kept his identity to himself, acting like a primitive life form as a means to test Luke, although he did promise to lead Luke to Yoda. He also warned Luke before returning to his hut that Luke must avoid the water as there were many dangers in the swamps of Dagobah. Upon Luke's arrival at the hut, Luke expressed his irritation at his not encountering Yoda yet, causing Yoda to voice his doubts to Obi-Wan Kenobi's ghost about whether training Luke was a good idea. Yoda reluctantly agreed to train him in the ways of the Force, after Luke realized the creature *was* Yoda and pledged to train under him, as well as Obi-Wan's reminder to Yoda that Obi-Wan himself was also reckless and impatient when he was younger. He expressed caution, though, as he sensed in Luke traits similar to his father and judged him too old for training.

 [![Yoda training Skywalker in concentration.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/YodaTrainingLuke-TESB40.png/revision/latest?cb=20211224041343) [![Yoda training Skywalker in concentration.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/YodaTrainingLuke-TESB40.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20211224041343)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/YodaTrainingLuke-TESB40.png/revision/latest?cb=20211224041343) 

Yoda training Skywalker in concentration.

 

The experienced Jedi Master expedited Luke Skywalker's Jedi training to fit in the limited time they could afford. At one point Yoda sent Luke Skywalker to fight the Dragonsnake King in order to humble the beast and casually reminisced with R2-D2 during the battle, before [using the Force](/wiki/Telekinesis/Legends "Telekinesis/Legends") to help the droid avoid harm and strike the beast with electricity - this was later shown to be a ploy by the old Grandmaster to ensure the beast would be dethroned as it was too large and powerful and had unbalanced the ecosystem.[[80]](#cite_note-Treasure-80) Yoda taught Luke new ways of using the Force, such as [short-term memory enhantment](/wiki/Short-term_memory_enhancement "Short-term memory enhancement"),[[81]](#cite_note-:0-81) and deepening Luke’s telekinetic abilities. During the training, Yoda also told Luke about his father's [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Mortis/Legends "Mission to Mortis/Legends") to [Mortis](/wiki/Mortis/Legends "Mortis/Legends"), in which Anakin, having seen his future shown to him by the [Son](/wiki/Son/Legends "Son/Legends"), was unable to resist the temptations of the dark side.[[82]](#cite_note-Fate_of_the_Jedi:_Apocalypse-82)[[83]](#cite_note-Ghosts_of_Mortis-83) However, prior to finishing his instruction, Luke chose to leave Dagobah without completing his training in order to confront Darth Vader at [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City/Legends "Cloud City/Legends") above [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin/Legends "Bespin/Legends") and save his friends. Yoda and the spirit of Obi-Wan Kenobi attempted to convince him to stay, thinking Luke ready to face neither Vader nor the revelation to come. Skywalker promised to come back in order to complete his training. Obi-Wan was concerned about this decision, telling Yoda that Luke was their last hope. Yoda quickly reminded Kenobi that hope still remained in the person of "another,"[[4]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_V:_The_Empire_Strikes_Back-4) namely Leia Organa, Luke's sister.[[2]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_VI:_Return_of_the_Jedi-2)

Afterwards, Yoda reflected on the events that led to that point. Although he knew that the Jedi Council was all but gone, and that his own age meant he would soon die, he nonetheless was still a Jedi Master, and even during the Dark Times, he believed the struggle would continue, with droids and aliens such as R2-D2 and Chewbacca, respectively, fighting the Empire. He also noted that Leia Organa, one of the leaders of the Rebel Alliance, resembled her mother, Padmé Amidala, and noted that an imprint on the parent was always strong. However, he grew concerned regarding Luke and Vader, noting that the imprint was not always a good path, and that Luke could become an agent of evil should he follow the same path as his father. But he also noted that Luke was both strong and good-hearted, which might mean that not only would he not turn to the dark side, but also that Anakin Skywalker might be redeemed. He then proclaimed his faith in the light side and the return of the Jedi Knights.[[84]](#cite_note-Power_of_the_Force-84)

#### Death[]

:   "*Twilight is upon me, and soon night must fall. That is the way of things, the way of the Force.*"
:   ―Yoda, to Luke Skywalker, shortly before his death[[2]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_VI:_Return_of_the_Jedi-2)

 [![Yoda becomes one with .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/YodasDeath-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20130402045854) [![Yoda becomes one with .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/YodasDeath-ROTJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130402045854)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/YodasDeath-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20130402045854) 

Yoda becomes one with [the Force](/wiki/The_Force/Legends "The Force/Legends").

 

When Luke returned a year later, Yoda had grown sick and weak, and knew his death was imminent. He informed Luke that his training was complete, but that his final test would be to face Darth Vader. He proceeded to confirm that Darth Vader was his true father, and scolded him for recklessly fighting Vader on Cloud City. He also told Luke that he should not underestimate Darth Sidious, and that he should pass on what he had learned, as the Force ran strong within Luke's family. With his final breaths, Yoda struggled to tell Luke his final words: "Luke. There is another Skywalker."

Yoda then died and dissipated as he became one with the Force. Darth Sidious eventually discovered Yoda's demise by probing Luke's mind when he was brought aboard the second Death Star, and proceeded to mock the deceased Jedi Master, while Vader reacted without any emotion at the news.[[64]](#cite_note-ROTJn-64) At the celebration after the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor/Legends "Battle of Endor/Legends"), Luke would look upon the [specters](/wiki/Force_ghost/Legends "Force ghost/Legends") of Yoda, Obi-Wan, and his redeemed father.[[2]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_VI:_Return_of_the_Jedi-2)

### Legacy[]

:   "*When you look at the dark side, careful you must be; For the dark side looks back.*"
:   ―Yoda to [Whie Malreaux](/wiki/Whie_Malreaux/Legends "Whie Malreaux/Legends") and [Tallisibeth Enwandung-Esterhazy](/wiki/Tallisibeth_Enwandung-Esterhazy "Tallisibeth Enwandung-Esterhazy")[[11]](#cite_note-Yoda:_Dark_Rendezvous-11)

 [![Yoda as a Force ghost](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008104501) [![Yoda as a Force ghost](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201008104501)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008104501) 

Yoda as a Force ghost

 

Doubtlessly, Yoda was one of the most gifted Force users in the history of the Jedi Order. Aside from his mastery of the Force, his most noticeable attributes were leadership and a very long lifespan. With almost a millennium of life, Yoda was able to establish himself as the most venerated Jedi Master throughout the entire Order—a status that would remain solely his for centuries until the fall of the Republic. As the reigning Grand Master for many centuries, Yoda had essentially become the "face" of the Jedi. As [Etain Tur-Mukan](/wiki/Etain_Tur-Mukan "Etain Tur-Mukan") mused, "Yoda was the Jedi Order," making it impossible to criticize him without sounding blasphemous.

Ironically, in this regard, Yoda had more in common with his Sith counterpart, Darth Sidious, than he realized. As Sidious was regarded as the vital and infallible leader of the Sith, so too was Master Yoda the vital and infallible leader of the Jedi Order. Thus, neither Yoda or Sidious could be criticized without their critics being automatically discredited and regarded with suspicion.

 [![Pic had unknowingly found Yoda's lightsaber while kidnapping Qu Rahn.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Pic.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080403145735) [![Pic had unknowingly found Yoda's lightsaber while kidnapping Qu Rahn.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Pic.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20080403145735)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8c/Pic.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080403145735) 

Pic had unknowingly found Yoda's lightsaber while kidnapping Qu Rahn.

 

In [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY/Legends "5 ABY/Legends"), when [Pic](/wiki/Picaroon_C._Boodle "Picaroon C. Boodle") and [Gorc](/wiki/Gorc "Gorc") were sent to kidnap [Qu Rahn](/wiki/Qu_Rahn/Legends "Qu Rahn/Legends"), Pic noticed an old silver-hilt lightsaber, which, although only Rahn knew at the time, had once belonged to Grand Master Yoda. Pic placed weapon on his belt and later used it to fight Kyle Katarn.[[85]](#cite_note-DF2-85) Pic's body was left by Katarn on the *Sulon Star* along with Gorc's; Kyle did not realize at the time that the tiny [darksider](/wiki/Darksider "Darksider") carried a weapon which had once belonged to Master Yoda. Later, after realizing the importance of the saber, [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker/Legends "Luke Skywalker/Legends") sent a group of Jedi to retrieve the lightsaber, though it was unknown if they succeeded; the weapon and Pic's body could have stayed intact on the ship, or someone else might have taken it.[[86]](#cite_note-WOTC5-86)

After his death at the age of 900, Yoda retained his individuality in the Force. As a so-called Force ghost, he would look down on Leia and the Solo twins when they were born. His teachings would become the basis for what Luke taught his [New Jedi Order](/wiki/New_Jedi_Order "New Jedi Order"). Since Yoda's teachings to Luke were rushed, most teachings of the Jedi Order were lost until the New Jedi Order began to find ancient holocrons, or, in some cases, libraries like the one on [Ossus](/wiki/Ossus/Legends "Ossus/Legends").

Yoda's ghost manifested on Coruscant for the birth of Jacen and Jaina.[[87]](#cite_note-The_Last_Command_1-87)

Yoda's power and wisdom impressed Luke throughout his life. Luke considered Yoda to have been wiser than himself or anyone else Luke had met.[[88]](#cite_note-The_New_Jedi_Order:_Force_Heretic_III:_Reunion-88)

As Yoda had informed Luke of the history of The Ones and their encounter with Obi-Wan and Anakin Skywalker during the Clone Wars when he taught the Skywalker, he contributed to the Jedi pursuit of Abeloth.[[89]](#cite_note-Apocalypse-89)

## Personality and traits[]

:   "*To be Jedi is to face the truth, and choose. Give off light, or darkness, Padawan. Be a candle, or the night, Padawan: but choose!*"
:   ―Yoda, to Whie Malreaux[[11]](#cite_note-Yoda:_Dark_Rendezvous-11)

 [![Yoda, respecter of all life, holds a  on his hand.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/Yoda-naturist.png/revision/latest?cb=20220908050817) [![Yoda, respecter of all life, holds a  on his hand.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/Yoda-naturist.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220908050817)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a7/Yoda-naturist.png/revision/latest?cb=20220908050817) 

Yoda, respecter of all life, holds a [neebray](/wiki/Neebray/Legends "Neebray/Legends") on his hand.

 

Yoda was the personification of what it meant to be a Jedi and a servant of the Jedi ideals. Yoda was the best equipped to guide the Jedi order. To his students, the elfin luminary Yoda could appear as either very strict or like a grandfatherly figure, testing them to mental and physical extremes one moment and showing warmth the next. Students often strongly disagreed with him at first, but gradually came to understand his attitudes. He believed strongly in the need to heed the insights of the Unifying Force,[[90]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Roleplaying_Game_Core_Rulebook-90) though he rejected the theory[[91]](#cite_note-The_New_Jedi_Order:_Traitor-91) the Force was essentially "grey."[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_novelization-65)

Among his colleagues on the Jedi High Council, he was known to have a penchant for mischief and practical jokes. To all of the young Jedi, he was the humble Yoda, who offered enlightened leadership and epitomized the ideals of the Jedi Order; a grand master of that august body, he was widely known as a sage instructor.

Although Yoda was a strict and firm leader, he deeply cared for the Jedi Order and the light side. The Jedi Master had the deepest commitment to the Force and the teachings thereof.[[79]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Sourcebook-79) Yoda respected Wookiees.[[92]](#cite_note-E3RotS3-92) He was willing to sacrifice a chance to win and neutralize Dooku by saving Anakin and Kenobi when Dooku unleashed an attack that would have killed them. Throughout the Clone Wars, Master Yoda showed concern for the lives of his soldiers as well as the state of the Republic and the Jedi Order.[[93]](#cite_note-The_Clone_Wars_Campaign_Guide-93) Yoda also greatly grieved Anakin Skywalker's fall and Order 66 killing almost all Jedi, to the point of falling to his knees. He was also willing to acknowledge whenever he was proven wrong, as shown by how he humbly apologized to Jinn—when the latter proved his unique wisdom was beneficial, as he had acquired the ability to retain identity—for having doubted him and acknowledged that he was a great Jedi.[[94]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Episode_III_—_Revenge_of_the_Sith_4-94)

During the Clone Wars, Yoda observed the strain the conflict placed on both the Jedi and the Republic. He considered that the Jedi, including himself, were becoming shortsighted and losing sight of their old ways, a development he regarded as troubling. He also recognized that the Republic had grown weakened by political division and self-interest, and following his [mission](/wiki/Battle_of_Thustra "Battle of Thustra") to [Thustra](/wiki/Thustra/Legends "Thustra/Legends") he began to doubt whether the costs of the war were justified, a matter on which he was no longer certain. At the same time, Yoda continued to regard the Republic’s founding principles as honorable, and he saw their defense as a duty he was bound to uphold.[[29]](#cite_note-JediYoda-29)

Despite a body of evidence to the contrary, which included famous names such as [Ulic Qel-Droma](/wiki/Ulic_Qel-Droma/Legends "Ulic Qel-Droma/Legends"), [Oss Wilum](/wiki/Oss_Wilum "Oss Wilum"), and [Revan](/wiki/Revan/Legends "Revan/Legends"), Yoda was largely a traditionalist in his belief that a Jedi who was seduced by the dark side of the Force would be forever condemned to walk in darkness. During the Clone Wars, however, he originally believed that no Jedi was beyond redemption and forgiveness. Even after Count Dooku betrayed the Republic and the Jedi by committing numerous atrocities as the Sith Lord Darth Tyranus, Yoda once tried to persuade his former student to let go of the dark side and return to the ways of the Jedi, and very nearly succeeded in redeeming Dooku. Even as Quinlan Vos slipped further into the dark side's embrace, Yoda had faith that the disturbed young Jedi Master would find his way back to the light side of the Force; unlike Dooku, Vos vindicated Yoda's belief in redemption.

However, Yoda's failure to redeem Dooku, as well as his inability to prevent the rise of the Galactic Empire, left the Grand Master more jaded than ever. In addition to the fall of the Republic, the Jedi Order was pushed to the brink of extinction by the fallen Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker, whose fall to the dark side turned him into the Sith Lord Darth Vader. Before his death, he warned Vader's son, Luke Skywalker, that "when a person falls to the dark side, their destiny would forever be dominated by darkness."

Yoda spoke an unusual version of [Basic](/wiki/Galactic_Basic_Standard/Legends "Galactic Basic Standard/Legends"). He tended to place verbs (especially auxiliaries) after the object and subject (an object-subject-verb format). An example of Yoda's speech pattern: "When nine hundred years old you reach, look as good you will not."([Listen](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5d/900YearsOld-ROTJ.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250408140228 "900YearsOld-ROTJ.flac") ([help](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Media_help "wikipedia:Wikipedia:Media help")·[info](/wiki/File:900YearsOld-ROTJ.flac "File:900YearsOld-ROTJ.flac"))) Most agreed that this pattern of speech was convoluted, and while it seems as though others of his species (e.g. Yaddle) had the same penchant for rearranging sentences, not all of them did (e.g. [Vandar Tokare](/wiki/Vandar_Tokare "Vandar Tokare")). As suggested by [Ben Skywalker](/wiki/Ben_Skywalker "Ben Skywalker"), he purposefully chose to speak like this so that people would have to listen attentively to what he said.[[95]](#cite_note-Backlash-95)

 [![](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Yodascrest.svg/revision/latest?cb=20120719090904) [![](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Yodascrest.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20120719090904)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/Yodascrest.svg/revision/latest?cb=20120719090904) 

[Yoda's crest](/wiki/Yoda%27s_crest "Yoda's crest")

 

Yoda walked with the aid of a cane later in life, although he was capable of throwing it aside and moving nimbly while using the Force. One of his canes was a gift from the Wookiees. His rare [gimer](/wiki/Gimer_bush "Gimer bush") cane contained nutrients that could sustain him were he to chew on it. He also used a [hoverchair](/wiki/Repulsorlift_chair/Legends "Repulsorlift chair/Legends") for moving around the Temple quickly and more efficiently.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25) Yoda was small enough to fit inside Luke's backpack, a fact which meant that Luke was required to carry him around during some of the Skywalker's training.[[4]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_V:_The_Empire_Strikes_Back-4)

Another item unique to Master Yoda was a [blissl](/wiki/Blissl/Legends "Blissl/Legends"), an instrument similar to a pan flute, which he wore around his neck while on Dagobah. During the Clone Wars, he would often make use of a kybuck given to him by a [Woolwarricca](/wiki/Woolwarricca "Woolwarricca") princess from Kashyyyk as a gift.[[96]](#cite_note-kybuckdatabank-96)
Yoda also had a unique [crest](/wiki/Yoda%27s_crest "Yoda's crest") that adorned his [quarters](/wiki/Yoda%27s_quarters/Legends "Yoda's quarters/Legends").

Yoda's origins were secretive and he never revealed his homeworld to anyone.[[97]](#cite_note-ultimateillustrated-97)

## Powers and abilities[]

:   "*Help you I can. Yes, mmm.*"  
    "*I don't think so. I'm looking for a great warrior.*"  
    "*Oh! Great warrior. Wars not make one great.*"
:   ―Yoda and Luke Skywalker, meeting on Dagobah[[4]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_V:_The_Empire_Strikes_Back-4)

Considered by many to be the greatest Jedi Master of the era, Yoda was one of the most skilled lightsaber duelists and users of the Force in the history of the galaxy. Yoda's powers awestruck even the Dark Jedi Beldorion, who grouped him among three elite Jedi Masters, along with Thon and Nomi Sunrider, who had lived several millennia earlier than him. Beldorion considered the trio to be truly great as they were prodigiously talented in the Force, specifically in the directing of pure light-side energies.[[17]](#cite_note-Planet_of_Twilight-17) Of all the Force users in the galaxy, only Darth Sidious, perhaps the most powerful Sith Lord of all time, rivaled Yoda's mastery of the Force and strength with a lightsaber.

### Lightsaber training[]

 [![Yoda was extremely skilled with the .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Air-Yoda.png/revision/latest?cb=20250414000724) [![Yoda was extremely skilled with the .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Air-Yoda.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/330?cb=20250414000724)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Air-Yoda.png/revision/latest?cb=20250414000724) 

Yoda was extremely skilled with the [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber/Legends "Lightsaber/Legends").

 

In addition to his immense connection to the Force, Yoda was amazingly skilled in [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat/Legends "Lightsaber combat/Legends"), one of the greatest duelists in history, and was widely acknowledged as being perhaps the greatest Jedi duelist and [Swordmaster](/wiki/Swordmaster "Swordmaster") of his time despite being trained as a [Jedi Consular](/wiki/Jedi_Consular "Jedi Consular"). He was known to be the only Jedi who could best both Mace Windu and [Count](/wiki/Count_of_Serenno/Legends "Count of Serenno/Legends") Dooku. Although he did not often participate in direct combat, Yoda's impeccable swordsmanship remained as sharp as ever. In his duel with Dooku, who had became Darth Tyranus and improved his skill even further, Yoda held the upper hand throughout the majority of the fight and would have defeated him had Tyranus not fled. Testament to his unnatural experience in dueling was that Dooku under his tutelage became a swordsman of rare skill and elegance, quickly rising to surpass most Jedi apart from Windu and Yoda himself. Nearly inconceivable was the last fight the small Jedi had against the leader of the CIS, which resulted in Dooku actually landing a hit (though minor) on the master of Ataru, a feat thought basically impossible to accomplish.
