Another testament to Yoda's immense dueling skill was that not only was he able to fight on equal footing with Darth Sidious, but he was also even able to defeat and disarm the Dark Lord, a feat that only Luke Skywalker (while empowered by the might and meditation of his family) and Mace Windu were ever able to replicate.[[74]](#cite_note-ROTS_junior_novel-74) In fact, Sidious was confused and confounded by Yoda's speed and skill.[[98]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Jedi_Battles-98) He was able to disarm Darth Sidious, who only preserved his life by throwing a huge blast of lightning Yoda had to cease his deathstrike to block with the Force,[[74]](#cite_note-ROTS_junior_novel-74) and then by shooting Yoda's saber from his hand when the Grandmaster was a moment too slow while maneuvering around the Senate chamber.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6) Overall, Yoda's mastery of lightsaber combat marked him as the greatest duelist of his time. Sidious himself, after having dueled Yoda, stated his belief that the [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master/Legends "Grand Master/Legends") would have "destroyed" Darth Vader if the young Sith had faced *him* rather than Kenobi on Mustafar.[[99]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord:_The_Rise_of_Darth_Vader-99)

Yoda received intensive training in the use of all the seven forms of lightsaber combat and had achieved full mastery and knowledge of them all and all of their stances and techniques. Known to be the best lightsaber instructor in the Temple, his complete mastery of each form was such that he was able to decide which one fitted his student the most and instruct them how to use their specialized form effectively. His most preferred style was [Form IV](/wiki/Form_IV/Legends "Form IV/Legends"), which he particularly specialized at, as it allowed him to compensate for his limited reach and stature. Known to be the Order's greatest master of Ataru, his technique was said to consist of the pure basics of Ataru taken to their highest possible levels.[[100]](#cite_note-Fightsaber:_Jedi_Lightsaber_Combat-100) Despite his advanced age and short stature, Yoda remained an exceptionally formidable duelist, displaying amazing speed and dexterity, leaping through the air and twirling as he battered at an opponent's defenses.[[72]](#cite_note-Labyrinth_of_Evil-72) Much of his lightsaber combat style relied on jumps and acrobatics, augmented by his mastery of [Force valor](/wiki/Force_valor "Force valor"). Yoda´s swordsmanship was second to none and allowed him to unleash a whirlwind of destruction upon his opponents. Fully utilizing his extensive Force reserves, Yoda could attack his foes from every angle possible, effectively surrounding his opponents singlehandedly in a barrage of strikes coming simultaneously in a 360 degree field. His speed especially was such that he seemed a blur to even venerated Jedi Masters, with only Darth Sidious ever being able to keep the tempo. Despite the fact that Yoda's primary combat specialization was Ataru, his skill in the form was such that he was capable of effectively overcoming it's weaknesses with ease and demonstrated an extreme level of skill with regard to deflecting blaster bolts and could easily handle many opponents at once, evidenced by his easy victory over many clone troopers when he returned to the Jedi Temple during Order 66.[[26]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Clone_Wars-26) In addition, Yoda at times applied his mastery of the other forms into his dueling style. He was known for having proficiently applied elements of Shii-Cho bladework and his outstanding deflection ability implied a superb level of skill in either Shien or Soresu.

However, in his later years, Yoda lost a great deal of his mobility, demonstrating a pronounced limp and depending on a cane to aid him in his everyday movements. This loss of mobility was due to the fact that, in his old age, Yoda suffered from debilitating arthritis.[[100]](#cite_note-Fightsaber:_Jedi_Lightsaber_Combat-100) When possible, Yoda preferred to use a hoverchair rather than walk at all.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25) His mastery of Force valor allowed him to overcome these physical infirmities, but due to the extremely taxing nature of the ability, he was only able to utilize it for a short time before tiring.[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_novelization-65) Even when he trained Luke Skywalker, however, Yoda retained enough skill to effortlessly defeating his pupil with only a stick, in spite of Skywalker being armed with a lightsaber and employing a [saber throw](/wiki/Telekinesis/Legends "Telekinesis/Legends") against him--and only lost when he allowed Skywalker to seize his stick.[[80]](#cite_note-Treasure-80)

Master Yoda carried a green-bladed [shoto](/wiki/Shoto_lightsaber/Legends "Shoto lightsaber/Legends"), which, unlike most other lightsabers, possessed an ignition button that also acted as a clip. Yoda was one of the few Force-users, Jedi and Sith alike, who kept his trademark homespun[[101]](#cite_note-SWCE-101) robe on during combat, possibly because it was small enough not to hinder his movements.

Yoda was able to cave his way through a host of [Spelunker probe droids](/wiki/Spelunker_probe_droid/Legends "Spelunker probe droid/Legends"), often moving faster than they could react or fire.[[102]](#cite_note-CW15-102)

Yoda fought his way to safety through a squad of clones during [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66/Legends "Order 66/Legends").[[92]](#cite_note-E3RotS3-92)

### Force powers[]

 [![Yoda demonstrates his ability to telekinetically move objects.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Yodaholdup.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20071004170841) [![Yoda demonstrates his ability to telekinetically move objects.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Yodaholdup.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20071004170841)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/1a/Yodaholdup.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20071004170841) 

Yoda demonstrates his ability to telekinetically move objects.

 

Yoda, as befitting a centuries-old Jedi Grand Master, was extraordinarily powerful and skilled in the Force, one of the most powerful Force users in history—rivaling Darth Sidious—and was the greatest and strongest master of the Force among the Jedi of his time, surpassing even the potentially more powerful Anakin Skywalker, due to having far more experience in using it. Luke Skywalker considered Yoda's powers to be far beyond what Darth Vader was capable of, and felt Yoda was likewise much more powerful than he was in 9 ABY.[[70]](#cite_note-HeirtotheEmpire-70)[[81]](#cite_note-:0-81) His power in the Force was described as being "as light as the stars." His midi-chlorian count was also known to be the second highest in the history of the Jedi, surpassed only by the Chosen One Anakin Skywalker. His strength and mastery of the Force was great enough that he could easily defend himself against and dominate other powerful masters of the Force, as shown when he casually repelled all of Dooku's Force assaults despite the increase in power and skill Dooku had acquired from turning to the dark side. Yoda was so powerful and skilled in Force combat that he could effortlessly overpower highly skilled and armed adversaries using nothing but the Force, as evidenced with Asaji Ventress. Indeed, Yoda was the only one to have ever managed to single-handedly go up against Darth Sidious in Force combat and matched the Dark Lord to a draw, although he proved incapable of defeating him as they were evenly matched. His power and skill in the Force remained tremendous even as he continued to age and lost his former great mobility. Even the Dark Lords of the Sith Darth Tyranus and Darth Sidious acknowledged his Force power and mastery, with Darth Tyranus holding his former master's strength in the Force in high enough regard that he believed that should Yoda fall to the dark side, he would be so powerful that not even Sidious would be able to stand against him.[[11]](#cite_note-Yoda:_Dark_Rendezvous-11) According to Luke, Yoda's powers far surpassed his own and Darth Vader's.[[70]](#cite_note-HeirtotheEmpire-70)

Master Yoda was extremely skilled in the use of mind-related powers. He could cast [mind tricks](/wiki/Mind_trick/Legends "Mind trick/Legends") that were easily strong enough to effectively manipulate strong-willed individuals, such as [Captain](/wiki/Captain/Legends "Captain/Legends") [Typho](/wiki/Gregar_Typho/Legends "Gregar Typho/Legends"),[[26]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Clone_Wars-26) and could easily delve deep into the minds of others to decipher their thoughts with great precision. Yoda's [telepathic](/wiki/Telepathy/Legends "Telepathy/Legends") capabilities also allowed him to manipulate the memories of his targets.

Yoda was also extraordinarily skilled in [telekinesis](/wiki/Telekinesis/Legends "Telekinesis/Legends"). He demonstrated on one occasion the ability to easily telekinetically lift and carry an [X-wing](/wiki/T-65_X-wing_starfighter/Legends "T-65 X-wing starfighter/Legends"), and during the Battle of Coruscant, he focused deeply in Serenity to raise an expansive force of Separatist destroyer droids into the air, ensuring that they would collide into the incoming airborne Separatist attack ships, which eliminated the two attack forces in one seamless stroke, then trembling with the effort and focus, he caused a pair of [C-9979 landing craft](/wiki/C-9979_landing_craft/Legends "C-9979 landing craft/Legends") to collide with each other on two separate occasions, first pushing some droids and Multi-Troop Transports back in and closing the doors, ere he made another landing one crash and blow them both up, then forcing two high in the sky to collide.[[103]](#cite_note-:1-103) In their duel on Geonosis, Yoda easily deflected every telekinetic assault from Darth Tyranus, who was a former Temple instructor of telekinesis. Yoda was able to catch Darth Sidious off guard with a Force-push that blasted Sidious away from him and later managed to stop a Senate Hoverpod that Sidious hurled at him from above, which he then proceeded to use the Force to throw back at him, an all the more impressive feat due to the fact that the pod was thrown upwards against gravity. He even could effortlessly toy with the very powerful Asajj Ventress, who was known to have defeated Kit Fisto and could hold her own against the likes of Mace Windu and Anakin Skywalker, using only telekinesis: he was able to easily send her flying, stop her strike in midair, and even go as far as to casually disarm her of her lightsabers with a simple gesture.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32) A master practitioner of the Force Push and [Force Wave](/wiki/Telekinesis/Legends#Force_Wave "Telekinesis/Legends") powers, Yoda used these abilities in conjunction with Mace Windu to blast away dozens of battle droids simultaneously during the Battle of Coruscant.[[103]](#cite_note-:1-103) Master Yoda was also adept at the saber throw, as demonstrated in his return to the Jedi Temple during the Great Jedi Purge.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

Yoda also displayed an astounding level of mastery in the use of the defensive power of [Tutaminis](/wiki/Tutaminis "Tutaminis"), using it during his duel with Darth Tyranus to effortlessly absorb and redirect the Sith Lord's Force lightning with no effort. Despite being nearly overwhelmed by its power, Yoda was ultimately able to absorb Sidious's lightning, eventually managing to coalesce the energy of the Dark Lord's Force lightning into a blue orb between the two of them, which slowly redirected the lightning back onto an astounded Sidious and caused him to slowly reel backwards with the strength of Yoda's counterattack before the combination of both of their Force powers blasted the two of them apart. Yoda also was able to use [Force Valor](/wiki/Force_valor "Force valor") to improve his physical attributes with the Force, and even after his exile was so strong in the Force that he was able to resist old age long enough to train Luke.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25)[[104]](#cite_note-The_Movie_Trilogy_Sourcebook-104) Yoda could, with great effort, use the Force to stifle and quash the efforts of his enemies to draw on the Force.[[105]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Miniatures-105) However, despite his great power and skill as a warrior, Yoda was known to strongly dislike combat in general, and was even a bit disdainful of the idea that "greatness" could be achieved through martial prowess.[[4]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_V:_The_Empire_Strikes_Back-4)

 [![Yoda could  overpowering  with his bare hands.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Yodasforcedeflection.png/revision/latest?cb=20130205191709) [![Yoda could  overpowering  with his bare hands.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Yodasforcedeflection.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130205191709)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Yodasforcedeflection.png/revision/latest?cb=20130205191709) 

Yoda could [absorb](/wiki/Tutaminis "Tutaminis") overpowering [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning/Legends "Force lightning/Legends") with his bare hands.

 

Master Yoda was able to [foresee](/wiki/Force_vision/Legends "Force vision/Legends") events with a great clarity, rivaling even that of Darth Sidious. In addition, Yoda had extremely strong [Force senses](/wiki/Force_sense/Legends "Force sense/Legends"), as he was able to quickly sense the deaths of almost all members of the Jedi Order and identify each one, while also sensing that Anakin Skywalker had turned to the dark side even all the way from Kashyyyk. Due to his training with Qui-Gon Jinn, Yoda acquired the power to retain his identity after becoming one with the Force.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6) He even was able to foresee that Luke would need to know about Mortis, an eventuality that came to pass more than forty years after the Jedi did.[[89]](#cite_note-Apocalypse-89) He was also able to ponder matters of the dark and light sides of the Force with unparalleled clarity that surpassed all other Jedi of his time, even Mace Windu. He was the most skilled user of [Force empathy](/wiki/Force_empathy/Legends "Force empathy/Legends") among the Jedi, exceeding even the renowned empathic abilities of Depa Billaba.[[106]](#cite_note-Power_of_the_Jedi_Sourcebook-106) He could sense intense feelings coming from others even from other planets, as he was able to sense the immense pain Anakin felt from the death of his mother, as well as hear the voice of Jinn's spirit, while the latter was on Tatooine even though Yoda was on Coruscant and meditating. He also easily sensed the tension between Kenobi and Anakin when they pursued Dooku and was able to identify the cause as Padmé's fall from an LAAT gunship.[[25]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones-25) Yoda [could see things far off](/wiki/Farsight/Legends "Farsight/Legends"), and had watched Luke through the Force for a long time.[[4]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_V:_The_Empire_Strikes_Back-4) Supposedly, he had a Force technique to guide humankind to be more moral.[[107]](#cite_note-Dark_Empire_1-107) Yoda could [enhance his memory](/wiki/Short-term_memory_enhancement "Short-term memory enhancement") and taught this power to Luke.[[81]](#cite_note-:0-81) He could also sometimes look through the eyes of other Jedi.[[72]](#cite_note-Labyrinth_of_Evil-72) Yoda could [stun](/wiki/Force_Stasis/Legends "Force Stasis/Legends") his foes, [change the environment](/wiki/Alter_Environment "Alter Environment") to try to block their attacks, [quash other's Force powers](/wiki/Force_suppression "Force suppression") and [make those not sensitive to the Force able to use it to a limited extent](/wiki/Enhance_Force_Sensitivity "Enhance Force Sensitivity"),[[108]](#cite_note-CotF-108) such as when his healing of Jorj Car'das made the man able to use the Force to a limited extent.[[68]](#cite_note-VotF-68)

Yoda could augment his body with the Force. One power he was fond of and used often was [Force jump](/wiki/Force_jump/Legends "Force jump/Legends") such as during the Battle of Coruscant, when even after floating a phalanx of destroyer droids into a flight of fighter craft and then twice straining himself to hurl entire troop landers to crash and burn into each other, he still leapt high and far to remount his steed.[[103]](#cite_note-:1-103) He used it again on the Wookiee homeworld to attack clones who were about to shoot him.[[6]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith-6)

Yoda was also quite proficient in the valued Force technique [Battle Meditation](/wiki/Battle_meditation/Legends "Battle meditation/Legends"), having even been able to determine the outcome of battles by lifting the morale of thousands of companions while simultaneously dampening the spirits of thousands of his opponents, wielding armies with the same ease as sabers.[[73]](#cite_note-The_Hidden_Enemy-73) Yoda could enter a [trance state](/wiki/Serenity_(trance) "Serenity (trance)"), then when he emerged his ability to use the Force briefly was more focused.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32) Moreover was able to summon the force power of [Emerald Lightning](/wiki/Electric_Judgment "Electric Judgment"), such as when he fought Darth Sidious,[[109]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars:_Who_Are_the_Jedi?-109)[[68]](#cite_note-VotF-68)[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Episode_III:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_novelization-65) and when he seeded it into a dark mirror of himself.[[61]](#cite_note-TCW:Destiny-61) In addition, Yoda could use [Force harmony](/wiki/Force_harmony "Force harmony") to defend himself from Dark powers and even shatter powers already in effect—this ability became more effective if Yoda was able to join his power with that of other Jedi.[[104]](#cite_note-The_Movie_Trilogy_Sourcebook-104) Yoda was believed by Luke to have, in 3 ABY, [used the Force to disable the sensors](/wiki/Ionize "Ionize") of the young Jedi's ship, then used the Force to guide the craft to where it needed to be.[[70]](#cite_note-HeirtotheEmpire-70) He was also capable of using it to inspire great amounts of hope while simultaneously eliminating feelings of doubt and despair from the spirit of others with a single touch, as he did to [saturate](/wiki/Inspire "Inspire") Palleus Chuff with feelings of hope and potential mission success while also completely dispersing his feelings of doubt and despair. Yoda was very proficient in the use of the Force to preserve life, having learned the use of many powers to [heal](/wiki/Force_healing/Legends "Force healing/Legends") himself and others,[[104]](#cite_note-The_Movie_Trilogy_Sourcebook-104) and even keeping himself alive though sheer willpower until he trained Luke Skywalker, though just before he allowed himself to pass into the Force he admitted he was at the end of his strength due to the great power required for such a feat. Upon his death, Yoda's body vanished as he became a [Force ghost](/wiki/Force_ghost/Legends "Force ghost/Legends").[[64]](#cite_note-ROTJn-64)

However, despite his advanced skill and power in the Force, he was only able to lift five of the seven [Muntuur stones](/wiki/Muntuur_stones "Muntuur stones") while in meditation once he passed his seven hundredth year.[[13]](#cite_note-The_Jedi_Path-13) Moreover, Yoda was aware of several [Sith spells](/wiki/Sith_sorcery/Legends "Sith sorcery/Legends")—though he did not use them, and understood the Dark Side powers to [kill with a touch](/wiki/Telekinesis/Legends#Force_Wound "Telekinesis/Legends") or take [total control over a victim](/wiki/Mind_trick/Legends#Mind_control "Mind trick/Legends"), though again he is not known to actually used these Dark Side powers.[[109]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars:_Who_Are_the_Jedi?-109)[[104]](#cite_note-The_Movie_Trilogy_Sourcebook-104) Yoda contemplated [using the dark side to remove all memory of himself](/wiki/Memory_rub/Legends "Memory rub/Legends") from a man, but ultimately decided that to do so would be wrong, and instead did what he felt the Force was guiding him to do and spared the historian.[[79]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Sourcebook-79)

### Other abilities[]

 [![Yoda in his hut on Dagobah](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/Yoda_TCGBtS.png/revision/latest?cb=20160925025410) [![Yoda in his hut on Dagobah](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/Yoda_TCGBtS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20160925025410)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0a/Yoda_TCGBtS.png/revision/latest?cb=20160925025410) 

Yoda in his hut on Dagobah

 

Unlike most other Jedi of his era, Master Yoda knew how to create Jedi holocrons. The diminutive Jedi Master created [at least one holocron](/wiki/Yoda%27s_holocron "Yoda's holocron"), through which he discussed various aspects of the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code/Legends "Jedi Code/Legends"). This particular holocron was rescued by [Jax Pavan](/wiki/Jax_Pavan "Jax Pavan") during Vader's attack on the Jedi Temple.

Yoda was known for being the wisest and smartest Jedi of his time. He was an exceptional strategist, being a great contributor to the highest level of Jedi strategy, and was also an exceptional diplomat comparable with the likes of Obi-Wan Kenobi and Mace Windu. As such, many of the sage's missions during the Clone Wars were diplomatic in nature, and he prevented many battles from occurring, though some, as in the case of his missions to Vjun and Rugosa, ultimately descended into battle.[[11]](#cite_note-Yoda:_Dark_Rendezvous-11)[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32) Yoda later demonstrated his strategical aptitude by choosing Dagobah as his place of exile, using the strong dark-side presence around the cave representing the dark side to block the senses of Sidious and Vader.[[70]](#cite_note-HeirtotheEmpire-70) Yoda also came up with a plan to evade CIS fire when his ship was ambushed, ordering all escape pods to be launched so the droids would not know which one he was in.[[32]](#cite_note-Ambush-32) Despite at times offering help to others, he was able to avoid any confrontation with the Empire during his exile.

Yoda was a very capable leader, as Mace Windu passed on the mantle of the Master of the Order to him, and he also at times led many attacks during the Clone Wars to victory. He also had enough strength to carry a box with a gigantic [chaingun](/wiki/Chaingun/Legends "Chaingun/Legends"), this weapon he used to destroy a droid army in order to save a [planet](/wiki/Unidentified_planet_(Yoda%27s_charge) "Unidentified planet (Yoda's charge)").[[110]](#cite_note-A_Stranger_in_Town-110) He was confidant that he could destroy the droid attack on the Wookiees.[[111]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Episode_III_—_Revenge_of_the_Sith_2-111) Sometime during his exile, he was able to craft a new lightsaber.[[112]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Card_Game-112)

Although Yoda usually had his soldiers handle the piloting, when required to personally pilot a ship, he proved surprisingly capable, as evidenced when he was forced to travel alone to Dagobah: he single-handedly flew a starfighter without fail, avoiding any damage while piloting it. He could even enhance his piloting skills using the Force, allowing him to safely reach the planet where the Force Priestesses were when Artoo and the instruments on the ship malfunctioned while in a small, glowing, golden nebula.[[60]](#cite_note-TCW:Voices-60)[[61]](#cite_note-TCW:Destiny-61)[[62]](#cite_note-TCW:Sacrifice-62)

Yoda was perceptive with his physical senses as well as the Force, as shown when he was able to catch Luke Skywalker cheating during exercises. By his own admission, food Yoda prepared often tasted foul.[[80]](#cite_note-Treasure-80) However, Skywalker felt the old master's stews tasted good.[[70]](#cite_note-HeirtotheEmpire-70)

## Behind the scenes[]

 [![The original Yoda puppet from .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Yodaold2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240721135936) [![The original Yoda puppet from .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Yodaold2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721135936)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7c/Yodaold2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240721135936) 

The original Yoda puppet from [Episode I](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace").

 
 [![A CG version of Yoda from Episode I was created as a test during the animation process for .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/TPMCGYoda.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008200709) [![A CG version of Yoda from Episode I was created as a test during the animation process for .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/TPMCGYoda.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111008200709)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/89/TPMCGYoda.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111008200709) 

A CG version of Yoda from Episode I was created as a test during the animation process for [Episode III](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith").

 

Yoda was voiced by Muppeteer [Frank Oz](/wiki/Frank_Oz "Frank Oz") in the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* films. In the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy") and [*The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), he was realized as a [puppet](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Puppet "wikipedia:Puppet") (controlled by Oz). Yoda's appearance was originally designed by British makeup artist [Stuart Freeborn](/wiki/Stuart_Freeborn "Stuart Freeborn"), who based Yoda's face partly on his own and partly on [Albert Einstein's](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Albert_Einstein "wikipedia:Albert Einstein"). In *The Phantom Menace* the actor [Warwick Davis](/wiki/Warwick_Davis "Warwick Davis") played Yoda for scenes where the character was required to walk. Rendered with computer animation in [*Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones") and [*Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith"), Yoda appeared in ways not previously possible, including his participation in elaborate fight scenes. However, Yoda's first appearance as a completely CG-rendered image was in *The Phantom Menace*, at the close of the film where he talks with Obi-Wan about his and Anakin's futures.

For the radio dramatizations of *The Empire Strikes Back* and *Return of the Jedi*, he was voiced by veteran character actor [John Lithgow](/wiki/John_Lithgow "John Lithgow"). [Tom Kane](/wiki/Tom_Kane "Tom Kane") provided Yoda's voice for both the [*Clone Wars*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: Clone Wars") animated series and [*The Clone Wars*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars") 3D series, as well as many video-game incarnations: *[Star Wars: Episode I Jedi Power Battles](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_Jedi_Power_Battles "Star Wars: Episode I Jedi Power Battles")*, *[Star Wars: Galactic Battlegrounds](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Battlegrounds "Star Wars: Galactic Battlegrounds")*, *[Star Wars: Super Bombad Racing](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Super_Bombad_Racing "Star Wars: Super Bombad Racing")*, *[Star Wars: Jedi Starfighter](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Jedi_Starfighter "Star Wars: Jedi Starfighter")*, [*Star Wars: The Clone Wars*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars_(video_game) "Star Wars: The Clone Wars (video game)"), *[Star Wars: Rogue Squadron III: Rebel Strike](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Rogue_Squadron_III:_Rebel_Strike "Star Wars: Rogue Squadron III: Rebel Strike")*, *[Star Wars: Battlefront](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Battlefront "Star Wars: Battlefront")*, *[Star Wars: Battlefront II](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Battlefront_II "Star Wars: Battlefront II")*, *[Star Wars: Republic Commando](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Republic_Commando "Star Wars: Republic Commando")* and [*Star Wars Episode III: Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith_(video_game) "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith (video game)").

Along with a few substitute voice actors in the original trilogy, but from the second one onwards, Yoda is dubbed in Japanese by the late [Ichirō Nagai](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ichir%C5%8D_Nagai "wikipedia:Ichirō Nagai"). By this proxy along with his and Darth Vader's appearance in [Soulcalibur IV](/wiki/Soulcalibur_IV "Soulcalibur IV"), Nagai also provided Yoda's voice in the Japanese version of the game.

The depiction of the number of Yoda's toes is inconsistent between different films, alternately numbering three, four and five toes. [Leland Chee](/wiki/Leland_Chee "Leland Chee"), keeper of the [Holocron continuity database](/wiki/Holocron_continuity_database "Holocron continuity database"), has stated that Yoda canonically has four toes—three in the front and one in the back.[[113]](#cite_note-Insider122AskLobot-113) For more, see the article on [Yoda's species](/wiki/Yoda%27s_species/Legends#Number_of_toes "Yoda's species/Legends").

 [![Very early concept art of Yoda](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/YodaConceptArt.png/revision/latest?cb=20230614033246) [![Very early concept art of Yoda](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/YodaConceptArt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/175?cb=20230614033246)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/YodaConceptArt.png/revision/latest?cb=20230614033246) 

Very early concept art of Yoda

 

Yoda's popularity is such that the comedy musician ["Weird Al" Yankovic](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/%22Weird_Al%22_Yankovic "wikipedia:\"Weird Al\" Yankovic") parodied the song "[Lola](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lola_(song) "wikipedia:Lola (song)")" with a version called "[Yoda](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yoda_(song) "wikipedia:Yoda (song)")," included on the album *[Dare to Be Stupid](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dare_to_Be_Stupid "wikipedia:Dare to Be Stupid")* (1985). More recently, [the Great Luke Ski](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luke_Ski "wikipedia:Luke Ski") parodied the song ["YMCA"](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/YMCA_(song) "wikipedia:YMCA (song)") by [the Village People](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Village_People "wikipedia:Village People") with a version called "Y.O.D.A." included on the albums *Fanboys 'n Da Hood* (1996) and *Carpe Dementia* (1999).

Producer/director [Mel Brooks](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mel_Brooks "wikipedia:Mel Brooks") lampooned Yoda in his 1987 movie *[Spaceballs](https://spaceballs.fandom.com/wiki/Spaceballs "w:c:spaceballs:Spaceballs")*. Brooks portrayed a diminutive character named [Yogurt](https://spaceballs.fandom.com/wiki/Yogurt "w:c:spaceballs:Yogurt"), who specialized in manipulating a magical energy known as the [Schwartz](https://spaceballs.fandom.com/wiki/The_Schwartz "w:c:spaceballs:The Schwartz").
[Yoda](https://muppet.fandom.com/wiki/Yoda_Muppet "w:c:muppet:Yoda Muppet") also made a cameo in *[It's a Very Merry Muppet Christmas Movie](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/It%27s_a_Very_Merry_Muppet_Christmas_Movie "wikipedia:It's a Very Merry Muppet Christmas Movie")*, voiced by [Eric Jacobson](https://muppet.fandom.com/wiki/Eric_Jacobson "w:c:Muppet:Eric Jacobson"). Jacobson took over many of Frank Oz's Muppet roles.

Yoda also appears in a [hip-hop](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hip_hop "wikipedia:Hip hop") Yoda music video that can be accessed via the *Revenge of the Sith* DVD when you go to the Options menu, highlight the [THX](/wiki/THX "THX") logo, press 11, wait for the pause, press 3, wait for the pause, and finally press 8.

To get the animation team back in shape for their work on Episode III, Rob Coleman and his team replaced the footage of the Episode I Yoda puppet with their Episode III digital model as a test to see how far they could push his usual performance boundaries. This footage was released on the DVD, where it can be seen as part of "The Chosen One" featurette on Disc 2 of *Revenge of the Sith*. The footage has since appeared in the Blu-ray release of *The Phantom Menace*, replacing the puppet Yoda.

Original concept art showed Yoda as blue instead of the green that he ended up being, and he is depicted as blue in *The Empire Strikes Back* novelization (published before the film of *The Empire Strikes Back*) . In Marvel's [*Star Wars* (1977) 42](/wiki/Star_Wars_(1977)_42 "Star Wars (1977) 42"), Yoda also seems to be tinier than in his normal appearance.

 [![Artwork depicting Yoda keeping busy in his hut was used on children's lunchboxes](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/YodaScroll.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101029165818) [![Artwork depicting Yoda keeping busy in his hut was used on children's lunchboxes](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/YodaScroll.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20101029165818)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f9/YodaScroll.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101029165818) 

Artwork depicting Yoda keeping busy in his hut was used on children's lunchboxes

 

In some foreign dubs of the films, Yoda's bizarre manner of speaking has not been translated.

In *[Before the Storm](/wiki/Before_the_Storm "Before the Storm")*, Luke Skywalker tells [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo/Legends "Han Solo/Legends") that when he first met Yoda, he was a hermit on Dagobah for a hundred years or more. The [prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy")'s storyline, created several years later, shows that Yoda was on Dagobah for no more than 22 years when Luke first met him.

*[Heir to the Empire](/wiki/Heir_to_the_Empire "Heir to the Empire")* and *[Vision of the Future](/wiki/Vision_of_the_Future "Vision of the Future")* describe how Yoda followed a Dark Jedi from [Bpfassh](/wiki/Bpfassh "Bpfassh") to Dagobah and killed him on the planet. After the [*Revenge of the Sith* novelization](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Revenge_of_the_Sith_(novelization) "Star Wars: Revenge of the Sith (novelization)") (which hints that Yoda had never been on Dagobah before his exile) was published, it has been suggested the battle occurred shortly after the exile.[[69]](#cite_note-holocron-69) In [*Star Wars Insider* 98](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider_98 "Star Wars Insider 98") [Leland Chee](/wiki/Leland_Chee "Leland Chee") wrote that the location of the battle is no longer considered part of continuity, but that it is possible that a mortally wounded Dark Jedi died on the planet after having fought Yoda elsewhere. However, this has not been confirmed.

Yoda received an updated character model to look more accurate to his *Revenge of the Sith* appearance for [The Clone Wars: Season Five](/wiki/The_Clone_Wars:_Season_Five "The Clone Wars: Season Five").

In the ride *[Star Tours: The Adventures Continue](/wiki/Star_Tours:_The_Adventures_Continue "Star Tours: The Adventures Continue")*, Yoda was one of the characters helping the [StarSpeeder 1000](/wiki/StarSpeeder_1000 "StarSpeeder 1000") pilot safely deliver a Rebel spy to the [Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic/Legends "Alliance to Restore the Republic/Legends"). However, as he was not known to have interacted with the Rebel Alliance during this time, it is unknown whether this is canon.

In November 2013, a deleted scene for *Return of the Jedi* was found on the laserdisc edition of the film. The scene, taking place on Yoda's deathbed and presumably occurring when Luke learns Vader was indeed his father, had him revealing that Obi-Wan Kenobi would have told Luke about his paternal relation to Vader had Yoda let him, making clear that Yoda was largely the reason Kenobi hid the truth from Luke.[[114]](#cite_note-Kenobi_redeemed-114)

 [![Yoda's signature in The Jedi Path](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Yodasign.png/revision/latest?cb=20120109122214) [![Yoda's signature in The Jedi Path](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Yodasign.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20120109122214)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Yodasign.png/revision/latest?cb=20120109122214) 

Yoda's signature in *The Jedi Path*

 

Yoda's signature in [*The Jedi Path*](/wiki/The_Jedi_Path:_A_Manual_for_Students_of_the_Force_(real-life_book) "The Jedi Path: A Manual for Students of the Force (real-life book)") differs[[13]](#cite_note-The_Jedi_Path-13) from that of the 1980 Yoda postcard made by Frank Oz.[[115]](#cite_note-Yoda_postcard-115)

### Non-canon content[]

:   "*Sick and weak I have become, Elderly and tir'd, And yet, I ask thee: When nine hundred years thou hast, Shalt thou look better?*"
:   ―Yoda to Luke Skywalker[[116]](#cite_note-Jedi_Doth_Return-116)

 [![A drawing by Roan Novachez of how he imagined Yoda would look](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/YodaAsImaginedByRoanNovachez-ReturnOfThePadawan.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141023201608) [![A drawing by Roan Novachez of how he imagined Yoda would look](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/YodaAsImaginedByRoanNovachez-ReturnOfThePadawan.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20141023201608)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a4/YodaAsImaginedByRoanNovachez-ReturnOfThePadawan.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141023201608) 

A drawing by Roan Novachez of how he imagined Yoda would look

 

Official non-canon *Star Wars* works generally still portrayed Yoda as a wise and skilled Jedi Master, but often played up his more humorous traits.

In [Jeffrey Brown](/wiki/Jeffrey_Brown "Jeffrey Brown")'s [*Jedi Academy*](/wiki/Jedi_Academy_(novel) "Jedi Academy (novel)") books, Yoda is a top instructor at the [Jedi academy](/wiki/Jedi_academy "Jedi academy") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant/Legends "Coruscant/Legends"), but not the academy's principal. Approximately 700 years old, he provides students with important training on the deeper aspects of the Force, but sometimes says things that are humorous or downright strange. He almost always talks backwards and laughs a lot. [Roan Novachez](/wiki/Roan_Novachez "Roan Novachez"), a student recruited to the academy at a relatively late age, was surprised by Yoda's appearance and nature and initially suspected that Yoda was teaching instead of being a full-time Jedi Knight because he was going kind of senile. Later in the series, Yoda became the personal Jedi Master to the [Zabrak](/wiki/Zabrak/Legends "Zabrak/Legends") [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan/Legends "Padawan/Legends") [Cyrus](/wiki/Cyrus_(Jedi_Academy) "Cyrus (Jedi Academy)").

In *[William Shakespeare's The Empire Striketh Back: Star Wars Part the Fifth](/wiki/William_Shakespeare%27s_The_Empire_Striketh_Back:_Star_Wars_Part_the_Fifth "William Shakespeare's The Empire Striketh Back: Star Wars Part the Fifth")* and *[William Shakespeare's The Jedi Doth Return: Star Wars Part the Sixth](/wiki/William_Shakespeare%27s_The_Jedi_Doth_Return:_Star_Wars_Part_the_Sixth "William Shakespeare's The Jedi Doth Return: Star Wars Part the Sixth")*, Yoda is the only character to speak entirely in haiku.

*[LEGO Star Wars: The Yoda Chronicles](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars:_The_Yoda_Chronicles "LEGO Star Wars: The Yoda Chronicles")* features Yoda and focuses on events seen in the prequel era.

### Clone Wars: Infinities: What if the Father never rescued Anakin from the dark side?[]

After Anakin fell under the influence of the [Son](/wiki/Son/Legends "Son/Legends") from [Mortis](/wiki/Mortis "Mortis"), they both returned to the regular plane of the universe. Both Yoda and Palpatine sensed their arrival upon Coruscant. Because of this both Yoda and Palpatine called a temporary truce to stop Anakin, but Anakin proved too powerful for either of them and defeated them with relative ease. He then became even more powerful in the process, and proceeded to create a Force hurricane in the Senate building.[[117]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars_Magazine_7-117)
